發現：評審情感與同行評審持續時間之間存在弱但統計上顯著的負相關，這表明更積極的評審往往與較短的評審周期相關。與評估、結果以及影響和研究價值相關的方面顯示出與評審持續時間的相對較強的相關性。方面層級情感與評審持續時間之間的關係在不同的評審輪次中也顯著不同。<lb/>  
原創性/價值：本研究將同行評審報告的文本內容與評審過程的時間特徵聯繫起來。通過識別與評審持續時間更密切相關的評審方面，提供了證據，可能幫助作者優先考慮修訂，並協助評審者和編輯提高評審效率。研究結果有助於減輕同行評審的負擔，加速學術交流和知識傳播。

##### **Learning the ARTS of Search for Automated Discovery**
2606.21891v1 by Gurusha Juneja, Arnav Kumar Jain, Deepak Nathani, William Yang Wang, Xin Eric Wang

Scientific discovery can be formulated as an iterative search process over the space of hypotheses and experiments. Contemporary methods navigate this space using heuristics such as MCTS. These algorithms conflate the merit of a hypothesis with the quality of its experimental execution. A promising hypothesis with preliminary execution is therefore ranked below a modest hypothesis whose execution is refined. Moreover, prior methods prune the search logs as the search progresses because the accumulated history outgrows the context window. We propose Agentic Reasoning for Tree Search (ARTS), where we deploy a reasoning language model to navigate this space. The model inspects prior execution logs, diagnoses whether earlier failures arose from faulty implementations or bad hypotheses, and selects the hypothesis to build on next. To mitigate challenges with context length, ARTS uses test-time training to instill the knowledge of search tree in the model weights. Across 22 tasks from MLGym and MLEBench, we show that ARTS outperforms leading algorithms, with over 15.3% relative improvement in the normalized score. With test-time training we show that a Qwen3-4B agent can match performance with closed-source frontier models like Gemini-3 Pro and GPT o3-reasoning with upto 5x lower inference cost. We further observe that on partially observable RL tasks, the test-time trained Qwen3-4B scientist surpasses ARTS with the o3 scientist by rediscovering the human-best recurrent-memory solution that heuristic methods prune away.

摘要：科學發現可以被表述為在假設和實驗空間中的迭代搜索過程。當代方法使用啟發式算法如 MCTS 來導航這個空間。這些算法將假設的價值與其實驗執行的質量混為一談。因此，一個有前景的假設在初步執行下的排名低於一個執行經過精煉的普通假設。此外，先前的方法在搜索進行時修剪搜索日誌，因為累積的歷史超出了上下文窗口。我們提出了樹搜索的代理推理（ARTS），在這裡我們部署了一個推理語言模型來導航這個空間。該模型檢查先前的執行日誌，診斷早期失敗是由於實現錯誤還是壞假設，並選擇下一個要構建的假設。為了減輕上下文長度的挑戰，ARTS 使用測試時訓練來將搜索樹的知識灌輸到模型權重中。在來自 MLGym 和 MLEBench 的 22 個任務中，我們顯示 ARTS 超越了領先的算法，標準化分數相對提高超過 15.3%。通過測試時訓練，我們顯示 Qwen3-4B 代理可以與封閉源前沿模型如 Gemini-3 Pro 和 GPT o3-reasoning 匹敵，推理成本降低至最多 5 倍。我們進一步觀察到，在部分可觀察的強化學習任務中，經過測試時訓練的 Qwen3-4B 科學家通過重新發現人類最佳的遞歸記憶解決方案，超越了 ARTS 與 o3 科學家，這些解決方案被啟發式方法修剪掉。

##### **TALAS: Teacher-Anchored Layer Alignment with Adaptive Sharpness-Aware Minimization for Embedding Distillation**
2606.21851v1 by Quoc Phong Dao, Hoang Son Nguyen, Pham Khanh Chi, Linh Ngo Van, Nguyen Thi Ngoc Diep, Thien Huu Nguyen, Trung Le

Knowledge Distillation (KD) has established itself as a pivotal technique for compressing large pre-trained language models. However, existing methods that force a student to strictly mimic the teacher's sentence embeddings or internal features often incur prohibitive computational costs and yield suboptimal performance due to the inherent capacity gap. To address these challenges, we propose TALAS (Teacher-Anchored Layer Alignment with Sharpness-aware minimization), a unified framework that synergizes hierarchical (multi-layer) alignment with robust optimization. First, we introduce a Teacher-Anchored mechanism that selectively distills final sentence embeddings only into the student's upper layers, thereby reducing overhead while respecting capacity constraints. Second, we bridge the semantic gap in lower layers via Layer-Aligned Self-Distillation, which propagates knowledge top-down using internal geometric relational constraints in the embedding space. Finally, to prevent the student from memorizing point-wise teacher noise, we integrate Adaptive Sharpness-Aware Minimization (ASAM) into the training objective, guiding the model towards flat minima for enhanced generalization. Empirical results on standard sentence embedding benchmarks demonstrate that TALAS consistently outperforms strong distillation baselines while achieving superior training efficiency in terms of computational cost and memory footprint.

摘要：知識蒸餾（KD）已確立為壓縮大型預訓練語言模型的關鍵技術。<lb/>然而，現有的方法強迫學生嚴格模仿教師的句子嵌入或內部特徵，往往會產生高昂的計算成本，並因固有的能力差距而導致次優的性能。<lb/>為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了TALAS（基於教師的層對齊與敏感度-aware最小化），這是一個統一框架，將分層（多層）對齊與穩健優化相結合。<lb/>首先，我們引入了一種基於教師的機制，僅將最終句子嵌入選擇性地蒸餾到學生的上層，從而在尊重能力限制的同時減少開銷。<lb/>其次，我們通過層對齊自我蒸餾來彌補下層的語義差距，這一過程使用嵌入空間中的內部幾何關係約束進行自上而下的知識傳播。<lb/>最後，為了防止學生記住逐點的教師噪聲，我們將自適應敏感度-aware最小化（ASAM）整合到訓練目標中，引導模型朝向平坦的最小值，以增強泛化能力。<lb/>在標準句子嵌入基準上的實證結果表明，TALAS在計算成本和內存佔用方面實現了優越的訓練效率，同時穩定地超越了強大的蒸餾基準。

##### **AgentCAT: Simulating Computerized Adaptive Testing via Multi-Agent Large Language Models**
2606.21832v1 by Weiyuan Zhou, Haiping Ma, Xiaoshan Yu, Changqian Wang, Shangshang Yang, Xingyi Zhang

Computerized Adaptive Testing (CAT), as a key technology for personalized education, aims to accurately assess examinee proficiency by retrieving exercises dynamically matching current ability estimates. However, existing CAT research is constrained by limitations of static offline data and isolated component optimization. Restricted by partial labels in offline logs, researchers degrade the dynamic assessment process into static sequence prediction. Current research focuses on isolated perspectives, e.g., selection or diagnosis, neglecting the overall CAT interaction process. To address this, we propose AgentCAT, a Large Language Model-based multi-agent simulation system, to construct a high-fidelity benchmarking environment for dynamic testing. This framework comprises three modules: (1) The examinee agent with memory retrieval and Chain-of-Thought reasoning simulates responses based on cognitive profiles; (2) The selection agent uses coarse-to-fine bucketing and knowledge graph exploration to balance local difficulty and global coverage; (3) The supervisor uses dual-auditing and robust update to ensure convergence and validity. To validate the framework, we evaluated on two real-world datasets across three dimensions: macro-level ability convergence, micro-level interaction logic, and data sparsity resilience. Results show AgentCAT achieves effective ability estimation, and its selection strategy balances difficulty adaptation and instructional coherence, aligning with human pedagogical intuition.

摘要：電腦自適應測試（CAT）作為個性化教育的關鍵技術，旨在通過動態檢索與當前能力估計相匹配的練習，準確評估考生的能力。然而，現有的CAT研究受到靜態離線數據和孤立組件優化的限制。由於離線日誌中的部分標籤限制，研究人員將動態評估過程降級為靜態序列預測。目前的研究專注於孤立的視角，例如選擇或診斷，忽略了整體CAT互動過程。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了AgentCAT，一個基於大型語言模型的多代理模擬系統，以構建高保真度的動態測試基準環境。該框架包括三個模塊：（1）考生代理使用記憶檢索和思維鏈推理，根據認知檔案模擬反應；（2）選擇代理使用粗到細的分桶和知識圖譜探索，以平衡局部難度和全局覆蓋；（3）監督者使用雙重審計和穩健更新，以確保收斂性和有效性。為了驗證該框架，我們在三個維度上對兩個真實世界數據集進行了評估：宏觀能力收斂、微觀互動邏輯和數據稀疏性韌性。結果顯示，AgentCAT實現了有效的能力估計，其選擇策略平衡了難度適應和教學一致性，符合人類的教學直覺。

##### **Test-Time Training with Next-Token Prediction**
2606.21803v1 by Xuan Ouyang, Zefan Cai, Junjie Hu

Next-token prediction is the self-supervised signal that trains language models, and every observed prompt token provides the same signal at test time. We study whether this signal can define the inner-loop objective for test-time training (TTT) in pretrained long-context language models. Many TTT architectures require models to be trained with test-time adaptation in mind, limiting their direct applicability to released LLM checkpoints. While recent in-place TTT methods make fast-weight adaptation possible for pretrained LLMs without redesigning the backbone, they leave a central question unresolved: what should each test-time write store? Existing recipes train the fast weight to match a learned local value proxy but they are not directly tied to the self-supervised next-token prediction signal. We introduce Test-Time Training with Next-Token Prediction (TTT-NTP), a drop-in fast-weight adaptation method for pretrained LLMs that instead supervises updates using the model's own next contextual hidden state. This makes each local write follow the same causal computation that supports next-token prediction: the value target is a pointwise linear projection of a single next-position contextual state. On RULER Full-13 (averaged over 4k, 8k, 16k, and 32k context lengths), TTT-NTP is the only method that consistently improves the released backbone across four models spanning three families and a 0.6--8B size range: Llama-3.1-8B (+3.9), Mistral-7B-v0.3 (+3.0), and the Qwen3 series (Qwen3-4B +4.1, Qwen3-0.6B +2.9). On the real-world LongBench-v2 long-document QA benchmark, TTT-NTP improves over the base model on both Llama-3.1-8B (+5.6) and Mistral-7B-v0.3 (+3.7), while preserving commonsense and knowledge performance.

摘要：下一個標記的預測是訓練語言模型的自我監督信號，每個觀察到的提示標記在測試時提供相同的信號。我們研究這個信號是否可以定義預訓練長上下文語言模型的測試時訓練（TTT）內部目標。許多TTT架構要求模型在考慮測試時適應的情況下進行訓練，這限制了它們對已發布的LLM檢查點的直接適用性。雖然最近的就地TTT方法使得預訓練LLM的快速權重適應成為可能，而無需重新設計骨幹，但它們留下了一個核心問題未解決：每個測試時寫入存儲應該儲存什麼？現有的配方訓練快速權重以匹配學習到的局部值代理，但它們並未直接與自我監督的下一個標記預測信號相關聯。我們介紹了使用下一個標記預測的測試時訓練（TTT-NTP），這是一種針對預訓練LLM的快速權重適應方法，該方法使用模型自身的下一個上下文隱藏狀態來監督更新。這使得每個局部寫入遵循支持下一個標記預測的相同因果計算：值目標是一個單一下一位置上下文狀態的逐點線性投影。在RULER Full-13（在4k、8k、16k和32k上下文長度上平均）上，TTT-NTP是唯一一個在跨越三個家族和0.6--8B大小範圍的四個模型中持續改善已發布骨幹的方法：Llama-3.1-8B (+3.9)、Mistral-7B-v0.3 (+3.0)和Qwen3系列（Qwen3-4B +4.1，Qwen3-0.6B +2.9）。在現實世界的LongBench-v2長文檔QA基準上，TTT-NTP在Llama-3.1-8B (+5.6)和Mistral-7B-v0.3 (+3.7)上均優於基礎模型，同時保留了常識和知識性能。

##### **CalVerT: Augmenting Agents with Calibrated Verifier Telemetry Improves Action and Learning in Knowledge-Intensive Tasks**
2606.21777v1 by Ashwin Vinod, Ying Ding, Elias Stengel-Eskin

LLM agents in knowledge intensive question answering take retrieval and reasoning actions with incomplete knowledge about whether their current answer is uncertain, unsupported, or already complete. This produces two failure modes: committing to confident but unsupported answers, which hurts accuracy, and over-retrieving when the evidence in hand already suffices, resulting in wasted compute. To give agents a more complete picture of the state space they are operating in, we introduce calibrated verifier telemetry (CalVerT), which augments the agent's state with additional telemetry: a calibrated self-confidence score and a grounding verifier score. We show that CalVerT can improve agents in both training-free and training-based settings. On four QA benchmarks, we find that CalVerT raises F1 by triggering retrieval in cases where agents over-rely on parametric knowledge, while cutting redundant retrieval in cases where agents have sufficient context to answer. We show that CalVerT can augment existing QA frameworks without training. Moreover, CalVerT also improves trained systems: by simply augmenting an agent's state with telemetry, we observe improvements after reinforcement learning, as compared to an agent with identical training but no CalVerT telemetry.

摘要：LLM 代理在知識密集型問題回答中，對於其當前答案是否不確定、未被支持或已經完整，採取檢索和推理行動時，知識是有限的。<lb/>這產生了兩種失敗模式：堅持自信但未被支持的答案，這會損害準確性，以及在手頭證據已經足夠的情況下過度檢索，導致計算資源浪費。<lb/>為了讓代理對其運作的狀態空間有更全面的了解，我們引入了校準驗證者遙測（CalVerT），它通過額外的遙測來增強代理的狀態：一個校準的自信心分數和一個基礎驗證者分數。<lb/>我們展示了 CalVerT 可以在無需訓練和基於訓練的設置中改善代理。<lb/>在四個 QA 基準上，我們發現 CalVerT 通過在代理過度依賴參數知識的情況下觸發檢索，提高了 F1，同時在代理擁有足夠上下文以回答的情況下減少了冗餘檢索。<lb/>我們展示了 CalVerT 可以在不進行訓練的情況下增強現有的 QA 框架。<lb/>此外，CalVerT 也改善了經過訓練的系統：通過簡單地用遙測增強代理的狀態，我們觀察到在強化學習後的改進，相較於具有相同訓練但沒有 CalVerT 遙測的代理。

##### **Hallucination as Context Drift: Synchronization Protocols for Multi-Agent LLM Systems**
2606.21666v1 by Carson Rodrigues

Multi-agent LLM systems routinely produce hallucinated outputs that cannot be explained by model deficiencies alone. A significant class of these failures arises not from model incapacity but from context drift: the divergence of internal knowledge states between concurrent agents. When agents enter a collaborative task with mismatched or stale representations of shared world state, their joint reasoning produces contradictions that manifest as hallucination. We define the Context Divergence Score (CDS), a lightweight scalar metric quantifying knowledge-state discrepancy between agent pairs across spatial, temporal, and task dimensions, and propose the Shared State Verification Protocol (SSVP), which lets agents periodically exchange compressed state summaries and flag high-divergence conditions before joint reasoning. We evaluate SSVP across two domains (multi-agent travel and software project planning) using Claude Haiku. In controlled experiments (n=30 per condition, travel; n=10, software) across 8 scenarios, naive full-broadcast synchronization increases hallucination rate by 34% above the no-sync baseline (HR: 0.658 vs. 0.492, p=0.0022, d=1.18), a contamination effect from propagating erroneous agent states. SSVP avoids this failure mode while showing modest, consistent reduction (HR: 0.463, d=0.30) and achieves significantly lower hallucination than full-broadcast (p=0.0005, d=1.47) using 58% fewer API calls. The contamination effect does not replicate in the software domain, where all conditions converge to low HR (<0.2), confirming it is specific to tasks where one erroneous shared belief cascades across evaluation dimensions. Our results reframe hallucination mitigation as a distributed systems problem and establish context synchronization as a first-class primitive in multi-agent LLM design.

摘要：多代理 LLM 系統經常產生無法僅用模型缺陷解釋的幻覺輸出。這些失敗的一個重要類別並非源於模型能力不足，而是來自於上下文漂移：並行代理之間內部知識狀態的偏差。當代理在共享世界狀態的表徵不匹配或過時的情況下進入協作任務時，他們的聯合推理會產生矛盾，這些矛盾表現為幻覺。我們定義了上下文偏差分數 (CDS)，這是一種輕量級的標量指標，用於量化代理對之間在空間、時間和任務維度上的知識狀態差異，並提出了共享狀態驗證協議 (SSVP)，該協議允許代理定期交換壓縮的狀態摘要，並在聯合推理之前標記高偏差條件。我們使用 Claude Haiku 在兩個領域（多代理旅行和軟體專案規劃）中評估 SSVP。在 8 個場景中的控制實驗中（每個條件 n=30，旅行；n=10，軟體），天真的全廣播同步使幻覺率比無同步基準提高了 34%（HR: 0.658 vs. 0.492, p=0.0022, d=1.18），這是由於錯誤代理狀態的傳播造成的污染效應。SSVP 避免了這種失敗模式，同時顯示出適度且一致的減少（HR: 0.463, d=0.30），並且使用 58% 更少的 API 調用達到顯著低於全廣播的幻覺率（p=0.0005, d=1.47）。在軟體領域中，污染效應並未重現，所有條件均收斂至低 HR (&lt;0.2)，確認這是特定於一個錯誤共享信念在評估維度中級聯的任務。我們的結果將幻覺緩解重新框架為一個分散式系統問題，並確立上下文同步為多代理 LLM 設計中的一級原語。

##### **When Is an LLM Worth It for Hyperparameter Optimization? A Budget-Matched Study on Tabular Data Finds the Warm-Start Is a Default Configuration, Not the Model**
2606.21641v1 by Carson Rodrigues, Oysturn Vas

Large language models (LLMs) have been proposed as hyperparameter-optimization (HPO) advisors that "warm-start" search from prior knowledge, proposing strong configurations in very few evaluations. We test that claim under a budget-matched, multi-seed protocol on eight PMLB tabular benchmarks, comparing an LLM advisor (LLM-OptFlow) against four classical baselines (random search, Optuna-TPE, Gaussian-process Bayesian optimization, and successive halving) over one shared search space, with paired tests and bootstrap 95% CIs across 8 x 5 = 40 (task, seed) units. The finding is cautionary. The advisor's strong first point is not an LLM output at all: like prior LLM-HPO systems the loop is seeded with a fixed default configuration, evaluated before any model call, which alone reaches 88.7% mean best-CV, identical to within 0.01 pp across all seven advisor models tested. The LLM's own proposals add only +0.40 pp of cross-validation accuracy over that seed and nothing on held-out test (LLM-Default = -0.01 pp, p = 0.92). When the same seed is granted to classical search, the apparent lead collapses: against seeded random search it leads by +0.20 pp at 2 evaluations, is tied by 5, and is behind by 12 (-0.37 pp). Without the seed, classical search ties the advisor by 12 evaluations and beats it by 40 (+0.6 to +0.8 pp, p <= 1e-4). Two LLM-specific behaviors survive: a single-task exploration failure (vehicle), and a rule-based confidence filter that removes ~33% of wasted compute without changing accuracy. The recommendation is deflationary: on tabular HPO, seed classical search with a sensible default; an LLM advisor adds no measurable generalization benefit and is overtaken within a handful of evaluations. We release the harness and a script that reproduces every statistic.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）被提出作為超參數優化（HPO）顧問，從先前的知識中「熱啟動」搜索，在極少的評估中提出強大的配置。<lb/>我們在八個 PMLB 表格基準上，根據預算匹配的多種種子協議測試該聲明，將 LLM 顧問（LLM-OptFlow）與四個經典基準（隨機搜索、Optuna-TPE、高斯過程貝葉斯優化和逐步減半）進行比較，這些基準在一個共享的搜索空間中，進行配對測試並在 8 x 5 = 40（任務，種子）單位上進行自助法 95% 置信區間的計算。<lb/>結果令人警惕。顧問的強大第一點根本不是 LLM 的輸出：與先前的 LLM-HPO 系統類似，這個循環是用固定的默認配置進行初始化，在任何模型調用之前進行評估，這單獨達到了 88.7% 的平均最佳交叉驗證，與所有七個測試的顧問模型之間的差異不超過 0.01 百分點。<lb/>LLM 自己的提議僅在該種子上增加了 +0.40 百分點的交叉驗證準確率，而在保留的測試中沒有任何增益（LLM-Default = -0.01 百分點，p = 0.92）。<lb/>當同樣的種子被賦予經典搜索時，明顯的領先地位崩潰：與種子隨機搜索相比，在 2 次評估中領先 +0.20 百分點，在 5 次時平手，而在 12 次時落後 -0.37 百分點。<lb/>沒有種子的情況下，經典搜索在 12 次評估中與顧問平手，並在 40 次評估中超過顧問 (+0.6 到 +0.8 百分點，p <= 1e-4)。<lb/>兩種 LLM 特有的行為仍然存在：單一任務探索失敗（車輛），以及一種基於規則的信心過濾器，該過濾器在不改變準確率的情況下去除約 33% 的浪費計算。<lb/>建議是貶值的：在表格 HPO 上，使用合理的默認值來種子經典搜索；LLM 顧問沒有增加可測量的泛化效益，並在幾次評估內被超越。<lb/>我們發布了這個工具和一個重現每個統計數據的腳本。

##### **Toward Open Weight Models Without Risks: Separating Public and Private Capabilities in LLMs**
2606.21638v1 by Charbel El Feghali, Arkil Patel, Nicholas Meade, Spandana Gella, Verna Dankers, Siva Reddy

Open-weight Large Language Models (LLMs) enable scientific progress and broad deployment. However, they make it difficult to control access to sensitive capabilities. Current practice either suppresses dangerous capabilities before release or mediates access through closed services that use specialized model variants, input/output monitors, and API permissions. The former is susceptible to jailbreaks while sacrificing capability for all users to mitigate the risks posed by a few, and the latter is fundamentally incompatible with open-weight release. In this paper, we propose Tiered Language Models (TLMs), where a single set of released weights supports multiple capability levels. In its default public configuration, a TLM behaves as a conventional LLM. A compact secret key specifies a permutation over a small parameter subset, inducing an alternative computation graph over the same weights that exposes additional capabilities. We develop a training protocol that jointly pretrains both configurations from scratch, then fine-tunes the keyed configuration on private data with regularization to preserve the public model's behavior. We pretrain 180M- and 650M-parameter TLMs and demonstrate that the keyed configuration can acquire a new language, gain instruction-following ability, and memorize private factual knowledge, whereas the public configuration exhibits none of these capabilities. Moreover, we show that our approach extends naturally to multiple hierarchical tiers. Because authorization operates on the model's weight structure rather than in the input space, the mechanism resists fine-tuning-based extraction and partial key compromise. In general, TLMs take a step toward reconciling open-weight release with selective capability control.

摘要：開放權重的大型語言模型（LLMs）促進了科學進步和廣泛部署。<lb/>然而，它們使得控制對敏感能力的訪問變得困難。<lb/>當前的做法要麼在發布前抑制危險能力，要麼通過使用專門模型變體、輸入/輸出監控和API權限的封閉服務來調解訪問。<lb/>前者容易受到越獄攻擊，同時犧牲所有用戶的能力以減輕少數人帶來的風險，而後者與開放權重的發布根本不兼容。<lb/>在本文中，我們提出了分層語言模型（TLMs），其中一組發布的權重支持多個能力級別。<lb/>在其默認公共配置中，TLM的行為類似於傳統的LLM。<lb/>一個緊湊的秘密密鑰指定了一小部分參數的排列，從而在相同的權重上引入了一個替代計算圖，揭示了額外的能力。<lb/>我們開發了一個訓練協議，從零開始共同預訓練這兩種配置，然後在私有數據上對帶密鑰的配置進行微調，並使用正則化來保留公共模型的行為。<lb/>我們預訓練了180M和650M參數的TLMs，並展示了帶密鑰的配置可以獲得一種新語言、獲得指令跟隨能力並記住私有事實知識，而公共配置則不具備這些能力。<lb/>此外，我們還展示了我們的方法自然地擴展到多個層級。<lb/>因為授權是在模型的權重結構上運作，而不是在輸入空間中，這一機制抵抗基於微調的提取和部分密鑰妥協。<lb/>總的來說，TLMs朝著將開放權重發布與選擇性能力控制調和邁出了一步。

##### **LLM and Human Modes of Representation**
2606.21616v1 by Shalom Lappin

Much work on the cognitive foundations of AI has focussed on comparisons between the ways in which Large Language Models (LLMs) and humans process information and represent it. One aspect of this comparison involves determining the extent to which LLMs can achieve or surpass human performance on a variety of cognitively interesting tasks. A second explores points of convergence and divergence between LLM and human systems for processing information. Here, I consider some recent research that has addressed both issues in two informational domains. The first is the representation of linguistic knowledge. The second is real world reasoning and planning. While LLMs frequently achieve impressive levels of performance and fluency on linguistic applications, they tend to handle linguistic content in ways that are distinct from human processing. They are also, for the most part, less efficient than humans in learning and generalisation for reasoning tasks.

摘要：許多關於人工智慧認知基礎的研究集中在大型語言模型（LLMs）與人類處理信息和表達信息的方式之間的比較上。這種比較的一個方面涉及確定LLMs在各種認知上有趣的任務中達到或超越人類表現的程度。第二個方面探討了LLM和人類系統在信息處理上的趨同和趨異點。在這裡，我考慮了一些最近的研究，這些研究在兩個信息領域中解決了這兩個問題。第一個是語言知識的表徵。第二個是真實世界的推理和規劃。雖然LLMs在語言應用上經常達到令人印象深刻的表現和流暢度，但它們處理語言內容的方式往往與人類的處理方式不同。在推理任務的學習和概括方面，它們在大多數情況下也不如人類高效。

##### **Cross-Modal Corroboration for Annotation-Free Wildlife Monitoring**
2606.21613v1 by Bharath Pillai, Varun Viswapriyan, Christopher Stewart, Tanya Berger-Wolf, Jenna Kline

Scaling wildlife monitoring for real-world conservation deployments requires automated analysis of smart sensors that operate under severe annotation scarcity. We propose leveraging expert knowledge of species activity patterns as an annotation-free validation signal for multimodal monitoring pipelines. We operationalize agreement as the alignment of independently derived hourly activity curves both with each other and with published behavioral priors-a three-way convergence that rules out shared-data confounds and dataset-internal correlation as alternative explanations. Our vision pipeline combines zero-shot species detection via BioCLIP 2, sliced inference to handle deployment-constrained camera positioning, and geometry-based geographic localization from camera trap imagery. Our acoustic pipeline detects species vocalizations via a fine-tuned classifier. We validate the pipeline on a breeding herd of Milu deer and demonstrate that both modalities independently recover activity patterns consistent with known deer behavioral ecology with minimal manual annotation. The framework applies to species detectable in both visual and acoustic modalities for which behavioral priors are documented in the literature, suggesting a practical path toward self-validating wildlife-monitoring pipelines at conservation scale.

摘要：擴大野生動物監測以應對現實世界的保護部署，需要對在嚴重標註稀缺的情況下運作的智能傳感器進行自動化分析。我們建議利用專家對物種活動模式的知識作為無需標註的驗證信號，來支持多模態監測管道。我們將一致性操作化為獨立推導的每小時活動曲線之間的對齊，這些曲線不僅彼此對齊，還與已發表的行為先驗相一致——這是一種三方收斂，排除了共享數據混淆和數據集內部相關性作為替代解釋。我們的視覺管道結合了通過 BioCLIP 2 的零樣本物種檢測、切片推理以處理受部署限制的相機定位，以及來自相機陷阱圖像的基於幾何的地理定位。我們的聲學管道通過經過微調的分類器檢測物種的聲音。我們在一群繁殖的梅鹿上驗證了該管道，並展示了這兩種模態獨立地恢復了與已知鹿類行為生態一致的活動模式，並且幾乎不需要手動標註。該框架適用於在文獻中有行為先驗記錄的可在視覺和聲學模態中檢測的物種，這表明了一條實用的道路，朝著在保護規模上自我驗證的野生動物監測管道邁進。

##### **ATLAS: Agentic Taxonomy of Large-Scale Software Ecosystems**
2606.21597v1 by Junyi Lu, Mengyao Lyu, Jiahui Wu, Lei Yu, Chengwei Liu, Fengjun Zhang, Li Yang, Chun Zuo, Yang Liu

The open-source ecosystem on GitHub lacks a systematic hierarchical taxonomy of software repositories. GitHub Topics, the dominant organizational mechanism, is flat, inconsistent, and covers only 67% of projects. We present ATLAS, the first framework that automatically constructs a hierarchical taxonomy for software repositories and classifies projects into it end-to-end. By combining LLM global knowledge with real repository distributions, ATLAS proposes meaningful splitting dimensions and iteratively corrects those that fail to accommodate real projects. A Designer Agent proposes splitting dimensions while a Classifier Agent assigns repositories; a self-corrective refinement loop uses classification failures to drive dimension revision through escalating strategies. We evaluate ATLAS on 54,387 GitHub repositories against six baselines spanning four paradigms, two downstream tasks, and three model families. On a stratified 2,001-repository benchmark, ATLAS achieves a Taxonomy Quality F-score (TQF) of 83.13%, outperforming the best baseline by 15 percentage points (on the full 54k corpus the approximate TQF is 73.0%, a gap driven by Path Granularity's all-or-nothing scoring on longer paths rather than lower classification accuracy). It is the only method to simultaneously achieve high structural quality and high practical applicability. On downstream tasks, ATLAS enables alternative discovery with P@1 = 85.71%, surpassing even human-curated lists (62.34%), and achieves the highest P@1 for repository retrieval. The taxonomy further reveals structural ecosystem trends that are difficult to obtain from flat tags or similarity methods: the shift from libraries to AI/ML applications (now 61% of newly community-adopted projects) becomes visible only through hierarchical, type-based categorization. An interactive taxonomy explorer is available at https://atlas-taxonomy.netlify.app/

摘要：開源生態系統在 GitHub 上缺乏系統化的軟體庫層級分類法。GitHub Topics，作為主要的組織機制，結構平坦、不一致，僅涵蓋 67% 的專案。我們提出了 ATLAS，這是第一個自動構建軟體庫層級分類法並將專案端到端分類的框架。通過結合 LLM 的全球知識與實際庫的分佈，ATLAS 提出了有意義的劃分維度，並迭代修正那些未能適應真實專案的維度。一個設計代理提出劃分維度，而一個分類代理則分配庫；一個自我修正的精煉循環利用分類失敗來推動維度修訂，通過逐步升級的策略進行。 我們在 54,387 個 GitHub 庫上評估 ATLAS，對比六個基準，涵蓋四個範式、兩個下游任務和三個模型系列。在一個分層的 2,001 個庫基準上，ATLAS 實現了 83.13% 的分類質量 F 分數 (TQF)，比最佳基準高出 15 個百分點（在完整的 54k 語料庫上，近似 TQF 為 73.0%，這一差距是由於 Path Granularity 在較長路徑上的全有或全無評分，而非較低的分類準確性）。它是唯一同時實現高結構質量和高實用性的方案。在下游任務中，ATLAS 使得替代發現成為可能，P@1 = 85.71%，甚至超越了人工策劃的清單（62.34%），並在庫檢索中實現了最高的 P@1。該分類法進一步揭示了從平面標籤或相似性方法中難以獲得的結構生態系趨勢：從庫到 AI/ML 應用的轉變（現在佔新社區採用專案的 61%）僅通過層級、基於類型的分類才能顯現。互動式分類法探索器可在 https://atlas-taxonomy.netlify.app/ 獲得。

##### **Per-Entity Bias Mapping for AI Visibility: Why Brand Mentions Require Entity-Specific Calibration**
2606.21595v1 by Zoltan Varga

AI-mediated answer systems increasingly determine how brands and organizations are represented to users. Existing approaches reduce visibility to mention rate or citation frequency. This paper argues that aggregate metrics are insufficient because entities exhibit systematically different AI visibility error profiles.
  We introduce Per-Entity Bias Mapping (PEBM): a ten-dimensional framework distinguishing raw from verified mentions. Three failure modes are identified: (1) underrepresented entities suffer invisibility due to weak knowledge graph presence; (2) large entities suffer the Brand Hallucination Paradox -- model familiarity creates stronger surfaces for plausible but incorrect completions; (3) CEE entities face a structural infrastructure gap across knowledge graphs, NER, and entity linking. A fourth dimension, Parametric-Retrieval Lag Asymmetry, describes divergence between retrieval-augmented and parametric memory update cycles.
  A full-scale empirical study (n=100 Hungarian B2B entities, 1,400 probe runs, 2,062 sources) finds Tier 1 brands produce 52.69% fabricated citations versus 37.87% for Tier 3 entities (+14.82 pp; p=1.67e-11), supporting the Brand Hallucination Paradox. Regulatory-framed queries elevate fabrication to 56.77% versus 37.59% baseline (+19.2 pp). We identify rejection-induced confabulation escalation: agentic quality filters function as hallucination accelerators in compliance contexts. We introduce ghost cartography as a unifying mechanism: entities in sparse latent regions produce confident output interpolated from neighboring dense regions, yielding a two-dimensional confabulation space (fabricated presence vs. frozen representation).

摘要：AI 驅動的回答系統越來越多地決定品牌和組織如何向用戶展示。現有的方法將可見性簡化為提及率或引用頻率。本文認為，總體指標是不足的，因為實體表現出系統性不同的 AI 可見性錯誤特徵。<lb/>  
我們介紹了每實體偏見映射（Per-Entity Bias Mapping, PEBM）：一個十維框架，區分原始提及和經過驗證的提及。識別出三種失敗模式：（1）被低估的實體因知識圖譜存在薄弱而遭受不可見性；（2）大型實體遭受品牌幻覺悖論——模型熟悉度為合理但不正確的完成創造了更強的表面；（3）CEE 實體面臨知識圖譜、命名實體識別（NER）和實體鏈接之間的結構性基礎設施差距。第四個維度，參數檢索延遲不對稱，描述了增強檢索和參數記憶更新周期之間的差異。<lb/>  
一項全面的實證研究（n=100 個匈牙利 B2B 實體，1,400 次探測運行，2,062 個來源）發現，Tier 1 品牌產生 52.69% 的虛假引用，而 Tier 3 實體為 37.87%（+14.82 pp；p=1.67e-11），支持品牌幻覺悖論。以監管框架的查詢將虛構提高到 56.77%，而基線為 37.59%（+19.2 pp）。我們識別出拒絕引起的虛構升級：在合規上下文中，代理質量過濾器作為幻覺加速器發揮作用。我們介紹了幽靈地圖學作為一個統一機制：位於稀疏潛在區域的實體產生從相鄰密集區域插值的自信輸出，產生一個二維虛構空間（虛構存在與靜止表徵）。

##### **Composing Verifiable Conceptual Models via Building Blocks: Towards Design-Time Verification of Agentic AI Workflows**
2606.21565v1 by Noe Y. Flandre, Alexander C. Nwala, Philippe J. Giabbanelli

Agentic AI systems orchestrate multiple LLM-based agents through workflow architectures that coordinate decisions, tools, and external actions. While current platforms emphasize runtime safeguards, little support exists for verifying workflows during system design. From a Modeling \& Simulation perspective, this gap is analogous to composing conceptual models without verifying whether their building blocks interact coherently. We propose a design-time verification approach that models agentic workflows as compositions of reusable building blocks and checks their compatibility through twelve structural rules. We implemented these rules in a software prototype and evaluated them using two openly released datasets: 48 workflows with known design flaws and 168 variants that preserve workflow logic but alter graph structure. Results show that our verifier reliably detects violations even when flawed designs are obscured through structural transformations such as splitting tasks between agents. Future works could combine our verification with community repositories of building blocks to compose safe agentic workflows.

摘要：代理 AI 系統通過協調決策、工具和外部行動的工作流程架構來協調多個基於 LLM 的代理。雖然當前平台強調運行時的安全措施，但在系統設計過程中幾乎沒有支持來驗證工作流程。從建模與模擬的角度來看，這一差距類似於在不驗證其組成部分是否協調互動的情況下組建概念模型。我們提出了一種設計時驗證方法，將代理工作流程建模為可重用組件的組合，並通過十二條結構規則檢查它們的兼容性。我們在一個軟體原型中實現了這些規則，並使用兩個公開釋放的數據集進行評估：48 個具有已知設計缺陷的工作流程和 168 個保留工作流程邏輯但改變圖形結構的變體。結果顯示，我們的驗證器即使在設計缺陷被結構轉換（例如在代理之間拆分任務）掩蓋的情況下，也能可靠地檢測到違規行為。未來的工作可以將我們的驗證與社區的組件庫結合起來，以組建安全的代理工作流程。

##### **Memory Is No Longer a Bottleneck: Memory-Efficient Graph Filtering for Scalable Collaborative Filtering**
2606.21540v1 by Jin-Duk Park, Won-Yong Shin

Graph convolutional networks (GCNs) have demonstrated significant success in capturing complex user-item relationships for collaborative filtering (CF). However, due to their reliance on extensive model training, training-free graph filtering (GF)-based CF methods have emerged as a promising alternative, offering computational efficiency by smoothing graph signals via matrix operations. In particular, polynomial GF-based approaches demonstrate improved accuracy through their ability to design more expressive and flexible filtering functions. Despite these advantages, existing GF methods suffer from a critical memory bottleneck: they necessitate storing the full item similarity graph, incurring prohibitive memory costs for large-scale datasets, which limits their practical applicability. To tackle this challenge, we propose Mem-GF (Memory-efficient GF), a new GF-based CF method that departs from conventional designs by principally leveraging the structure of Krylov subspaces as a core mechanism for approximating polynomial graph filters without explicitly storing the item similarity graph. We theoretically analyze the minimum Krylov subspace size that guarantees lossless approximation. Through extensive experiments, we demonstrate that Mem-GF achieves up to 5.74$\times$ lower memory usage and 4.38$\times$ speedup in runtime, while consistently exceeding the recommendation accuracy of state-of-the-art GF and GCN-based methods. Mem-GF robustly scales to datasets with tens of millions of interactions, establishing itself as a practically viable and theoretically grounded solution for efficient CF.

摘要：圖卷積網絡（GCNs）在捕捉複雜的用戶-項目關係以進行協同過濾（CF）方面取得了顯著成功。<lb/>然而，由於其依賴於廣泛的模型訓練，無需訓練的圖過濾（GF）基於CF的方法作為一種有前景的替代方案出現，通過矩陣運算平滑圖信號來提供計算效率。<lb/>特別是，多項式GF基礎的方法通過設計更具表達力和靈活性的過濾函數來提高準確性。<lb/>儘管這些優勢，現有的GF方法面臨一個關鍵的內存瓶頸：它們需要存儲完整的項目相似度圖，這對於大規模數據集來說會產生高昂的內存成本，限制了它們的實際應用性。<lb/>為了解決這一挑戰，我們提出了Mem-GF（內存高效GF），這是一種新的GF基礎CF方法，主要利用Krylov子空間的結構作為近似多項式圖過濾器的核心機制，而不需要明確存儲項目相似度圖。<lb/>我們從理論上分析了保證無損近似的最小Krylov子空間大小。<lb/>通過廣泛的實驗，我們證明Mem-GF在內存使用上降低了最多5.74$\times$，在運行時間上加速了4.38$\times$，同時持續超越最先進的GF和GCN基礎方法的推薦準確性。<lb/>Mem-GF穩健地擴展到具有數千萬次交互的數據集，確立了其作為一種實際可行且理論基礎的高效CF解決方案。

##### **MedHal-Loc: Are "Explainable-by-Architecture" Medical Hallucination Detectors Faithful Localizers? A Localization Benchmark**
2606.21517v1 by Minmin Chen, Daojian Lu, Yining Dai, Jvyu Cai, Fengdan Chen

Detecting hallucinations in clinical text is increasingly framed as an explainability problem: systems should not merely flag an unreliable response but point to the offending span. Architectures built around knowledge-graph (KG) triple decomposition are marketed for exactly this auditability, yet their localization ability is typically assumed rather than measured. We introduce MedHal-Loc, a benchmark and metric for localization faithfulness -- whether a detector's top-ranked error unit actually overlaps the erroneous span. The controlled subset comprises 300 PubMedQA-derived statements with single, span-level errors injected across four localizable types (entity substitution, relation error, mechanism misattribution, invention), yielding gold spans by construction; a complementary natural subset documents that real hallucinations are dominated by diffuse conclusion-flips that resist span localization (a human expert accepted 1/18 candidate spans). Evaluating four fine-grained paradigms, we find that NLI-per-clause, consistency-per-sentence, and the dedicated span detector FAVA all localize well above chance, whereas an elaborate KG-triple pipeline localizes no better than chance (+3.3pp, n.s.), bottlenecked by ~59% entity-extraction coverage -- despite competitive detection F1 (0.609). Detection competence does not imply faithful localization; architectural explainability must be validated, not presumed.

摘要：在臨床文本中檢測幻覺越來越被框架為一個可解釋性問題：系統不僅應該標記不可靠的回應，還應指向問題的範圍。圍繞知識圖譜（KG）三元組分解構建的架構正是為了這種可審計性而推廣，但它們的定位能力通常是被假設而不是測量的。我們引入了MedHal-Loc，一個針對定位忠實度的基準和指標——即檢測器的最高排名錯誤單元是否實際上與錯誤範圍重疊。受控子集包含300個來自PubMedQA的聲明，這些聲明在四種類型的可定位錯誤（實體替換、關係錯誤、機制錯誤歸因、發明）中注入了單一的範圍級錯誤，從而構建出金標範圍；一個補充的自然子集記錄了真實幻覺主要由抵抗範圍定位的擴散結論翻轉所主導（人類專家接受了18個候選範圍中的1個）。在評估四種細緻的範式時，我們發現NLI-per-clause、consistency-per-sentence和專用的範圍檢測器FAVA的定位效果均顯著高於隨機，而一個複雜的KG三元組管道的定位效果則不比隨機更好（+3.3pp，n.s.），其瓶頸在於約59%的實體提取覆蓋率——儘管檢測F1（0.609）具有競爭力。檢測能力並不意味著忠實的定位；架構的可解釋性必須經過驗證，而不是假定。

##### **Decoupling the Declarative from the Procedural in Vision-Language-Action Models**
2606.21496v1 by Nikolaos Tsagkas, Andreas Sochopoulos, Chris Xiaoxuan Lu, Oisin Mac Aodha, Alexandros Kouris

Deploying generalist robotic agents in the real world requires transferable skills. Specifically, a policy trained to clone a behavior from object-specific demonstrations must generalize beyond that object, otherwise data collection requirements become intractable. Recently, fine-tuning of pre-trained billion-parameter Vision-Language Models (VLMs), initially on large-scale robot datasets and then on fewer scenario-specific demonstrations, has emerged as the predominant paradigm for designing Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models. While these policies achieve state-of-the-art manipulation performance in-distribution, they remain brittle to minor spatial, semantic, and task variations. In this work, we address the inability of current models to decouple the declarative (i.e., concepts and entity semantics) from the procedural knowledge (i.e., how to do something) encoded in their parameters, which is a fundamental bottleneck for zero-shot skill transfer to novel objects. To address this, we propose w$^{2}$VLA, a new VLA model with restructured information flow. Rather than feeding all multimodal tokens from the VLM encoder into a large, opaque transformer-based action expert, our approach modulates the robot state sequence with visual, spatial, and skill information in a compositional and interpretable manner. Unlike popular, state-of-the-art VLAs, we show that our modular approach successfully decouples knowledge representations, enabling robust behavior cloning and unprecedented zero-shot skill transfer capabilities across dissimilar, unseen objects.

摘要：部署通用機器人代理於現實世界需要可轉移的技能。具體而言，從物體特定示範中訓練出來的策略必須能夠超越該物體進行概括，否則數據收集的需求將變得無法處理。最近，對預訓練的十億參數視覺-語言模型（VLMs）的微調，最初是在大規模機器人數據集上，然後在較少的場景特定示範上進行，已成為設計視覺-語言-行動（VLA）模型的主要範式。儘管這些策略在分佈內達到了最先進的操作性能，但對於輕微的空間、語義和任務變化仍然脆弱。在本研究中，我們解決了當前模型無法將陳述性知識（即概念和實體語義）與程序性知識（即如何做某事）從其參數中解耦的問題，這是對新物體進行零樣本技能轉移的根本瓶頸。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了w$^{2}$VLA，一種具有重構信息流的新VLA模型。我們的方法不是將來自VLM編碼器的所有多模態標記輸入到一個大型、不透明的基於Transformer的行動專家中，而是以組合和可解釋的方式調節機器人狀態序列，結合視覺、空間和技能信息。與流行的最先進VLA不同，我們展示了我們的模塊化方法成功地解耦了知識表示，實現了穩健的行為克隆和前所未有的零樣本技能轉移能力，適用於不同的、未見過的物體。

##### **Does Mixture-of-Experts Actually Help Inference on Consumer and Edge Hardware? An Empirical Study**
2606.21428v1 by Alfarizy Alfarizy, Hung Truong Thanh Nguyen, René Richard, Roozbeh Razavi-Far, Hung Cao

Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) language models are often described as ideal for resource-constrained inference. Each token activates only a small subset of experts, so the per-token compute cost, in floating-point operations (FLOPs), resembles that of a much smaller dense model. Whether that FLOP advantage survives in practice is far less clear. We ask whether MoE models actually run faster and cheaper than comparable dense models on consumer-grade and edge hardware. We benchmark OLMoE-1B-7B (1.3 B active of 6.9 B total) against three dense baselines on an Apple M2 Pro and an NVIDIA Jetson Orin Nano 8 GB through llama.cpp, measuring throughput, memory, and on-device energy. The answer is device-dependent: OLMoE's active-parameter advantage is only partly realised on the laptop (~10% behind the same-active Llama-3.2-1B) and erodes on the edge device (~31% behind, at 2.1$\times$ the energy per token, with peak memory at the 8 GB ceiling). Patching llama.cpp to time the decode graph node-by-node shows routing accounts for under 9% of MoE-block compute on the cleaner edge backend, so the gap reflects total-parameter memory footprint, expert dispatch, and KV-cache pressure rather than routing. The implication is that on bandwidth-bound edge hardware, inference cost tracks total parameters, not active ones, and sparse activation does not buy back what the device is constrained on. These findings are bounded to one MoE model at this parameter scale and two devices, and we release the full measurement harness and per-run data.

摘要：混合專家（MoE）語言模型通常被描述為在資源受限的推理中理想的選擇。每個標記僅激活一小部分專家，因此每個標記的計算成本，以浮點運算（FLOPs）來計算，類似於一個小得多的密集模型。這種FLOP優勢在實踐中是否依然存在則不太明確。我們詢問MoE模型是否實際上在消費級和邊緣硬體上運行得比可比的密集模型更快且更便宜。我們在Apple M2 Pro和NVIDIA Jetson Orin Nano 8 GB上通過llama.cpp基準測試OLMoE-1B-7B（1.3 B活躍的6.9 B總數）對三個密集基準進行測試，測量吞吐量、內存和設備內能耗。答案取決於設備：OLMoE的活躍參數優勢僅在筆記本電腦上部分實現（約比同時活躍的Llama-3.2-1B慢10%），在邊緣設備上則減少（約慢31%，每個標記的能耗為2.1$\times$，峰值內存達到8 GB的上限）。對llama.cpp進行修補以逐個節點計時解碼圖顯示，路由在更乾淨的邊緣後端中僅佔MoE區塊計算的不到9%，因此差距反映的是總參數的內存佔用、專家調度和KV緩存壓力，而不是路由。這意味著在帶寬受限的邊緣硬體上，推理成本與總參數相關，而不是活躍參數，稀疏激活並未彌補設備的限制。這些發現僅限於在此參數規模下的一個MoE模型和兩個設備，我們發布了完整的測量工具和每次運行的數據。

##### **Factual Retrieval in LLMs Is a Redundant, Distributed and Non-Contiguous Process**
2606.21345v1 by Hail Hochman, Natalie Shapira, Yoav Goldberg

Large language models (LLMs) store and recall factual knowledge, yet the precise mechanism of how entity representations are transformed to enable specific attribute retrieval remains underexplored. In this work, we investigate this mechanism through the lens of an "attribute-computation path"-a sequence of computational steps over the entity representation required to elicit a target attribute. We then propose an iterative patching protocol to identify a minimal subset of layers necessary for this computation. Applying our method to LLaMA 3.1 8B and Qwen3 8B, we find that these paths are non-contiguous, often skipping layers, and that models possess multiple, functionally-equivalent paths for the same entity and fact, highlighting a high degree of redundancy in attribute computation. This implies that knowledge computation is highly distributed, potentially explaining the localization-editing mismatch and suggesting that knowledge storage and retrieval in LLMs is far from being well understood.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）儲存並回憶事實知識，但如何將實體表示轉換以啟用特定屬性檢索的精確機制仍然未被充分探討。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們通過“屬性計算路徑”的視角來研究這一機制——這是一系列針對實體表示的計算步驟，旨在引出目標屬性。<lb/>然後，我們提出了一種迭代修補協議，以識別進行此計算所需的最小層次子集。<lb/>將我們的方法應用於 LLaMA 3.1 8B 和 Qwen3 8B 時，我們發現這些路徑是不連續的，經常跳過層次，並且模型對於相同的實體和事實擁有多條功能上等價的路徑，突顯了屬性計算中的高度冗餘。<lb/>這意味著知識計算是高度分散的，可能解釋了定位編輯不匹配的現象，並暗示 LLM 中的知識儲存和檢索遠未被充分理解。

##### **DataClaw0: Agentic Tailoring Multimodal Data from Raw Streams**
2606.21337v1 by Cong Wan, Zeyu Guo, Zijian Cai, Jiangyang Li, SongLin Dong, Lin Peng, Xiangyang Luo, Zhiheng Ma, Yihong Gong

Massive unstructured multimodal streams suffer from high "data entropy," impeding both efficient human knowledge acquisition and high-quality AI post-training. Existing passive annotation paradigms, heavily reliant on heuristic rules or general VLMs, are costly, monotonous, and fail to unlock the deep procedural logic embedded in raw data. We elevate data processing to a learnable capability, proposing a paradigm shift towards Agentic Data Tailoring, which actively refining and structuring data to align with diverse user and downstream intents. To overcome the data scarcity bottleneck in training such high-order capabilities, we design a two-stage pipeline grounding generative semantic synthesis in deterministic Factual Anchors, yielding a large-scale dataset spanning five core physical and digital domains. Building upon this, $\text{DataClaw}_0$-9B model synergizes Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), achieving robust alignment with complex refinement and tailoring intents. To systematically quantify this capability, we construct $\text{DataClaw}_0$-val, the first benchmark dedicated to data refinement. Crucially, we adopt downstream post-training as the ultimate validation touchstone. Evaluations on video generation, real-world VQA, and GUI navigation confirm that $\text{DataClaw}_0$ delivers high-information-density tailored data, facilitating efficient model adaptation to new tasks under limited training data regimes. Project page: https://czjdsg.github.io/MakeAnyData

摘要：大規模的非結構化多模態數據流遭受高「數據熵」的困擾，妨礙了高效的人類知識獲取和高品質的AI後訓練。現有的被動標註範式，過度依賴啟發式規則或通用的VLM，成本高昂、單調乏味，且未能解鎖原始數據中深層的程序邏輯。我們將數據處理提升為一種可學習的能力，提出一種向代理數據定制的範式轉變，主動地精煉和結構化數據，以符合多樣化的用戶和下游意圖。為了克服訓練此類高階能力中的數據稀缺瓶頸，我們設計了一個兩階段的管道，將生成語義合成基於確定性的事實錨點，產生一個涵蓋五個核心物理和數字領域的大規模數據集。在此基礎上，$\text{DataClaw}_0$-9B模型將監督微調（SFT）與群體相對政策優化（GRPO）協同，實現與複雜精煉和定制意圖的強健對齊。為了系統地量化這一能力，我們構建了$\text{DataClaw}_0$-val，這是首個專門針對數據精煉的基準。關鍵是，我們將下游後訓練作為最終的驗證基準。在視頻生成、現實世界VQA和GUI導航的評估中，確認$\text{DataClaw}_0$提供高信息密度的定制數據，促進模型在有限訓練數據環境下對新任務的高效適應。項目頁面：https://czjdsg.github.io/MakeAnyData

##### **Topological Neural Dynamics: A Neuron-wise Framework for Sequence Modeling**
2606.21295v1 by Borui Cai, Yao Zhao

Existing sequence models, including RNNs, LSTMs, continuous-time networks, and Transformers, share a common structural principle: layer-wise dynamics, where all neurons in the same layer co-evolve through a shared parameterized operator, leaving individual neurons no freedom to evolve independently. Yet in many complex dynamical systems, rich global behavior emerges precisely from locally evolving units interacting through structured connectivity. Inspired by this principle, we introduce Topological Neural Dynamics (TND), a sequence modeling framework that shifts computation from layer-wise to neuron-wise dynamics. TND represents a neural system as a directed neuron graph, an interaction operator, and a local dynamics function, where each neuron evolves independently and collective computation emerges from interactions through the explicit graph topology. We instantiate TND as a discrete-time graph-coupled dynamical system and evaluate it as a case study on a behavior cloning task in single-player Pong. Compared with Vanilla RNN, Sparse RNN, LSTM, Closed-form continuous-time neural network (CfC), and Transformer baselines, TND achieves the best catch rate and a mean of 17.47 consecutive catches per round, more than three times that of the strongest baseline. These results suggest that shifting from layer-wise to neuron-wise dynamics provides an effective inductive bias for sequence modeling.

摘要：現有的序列模型，包括RNN、LSTM、連續時間網絡和Transformer，具有共同的結構原則：層級動態，其中同一層的所有神經元通過共享的參數化運算子共同演化，使得個別神經元無法獨立演化。然而，在許多複雜的動態系統中，豐富的全局行為恰恰是由局部演化單元通過結構化連接互動而產生的。受到這一原則的啟發，我們引入了拓撲神經動態（TND），這是一種將計算從層級動態轉變為神經元動態的序列建模框架。TND將神經系統表示為一個有向神經元圖、一個互動運算子和一個局部動態函數，其中每個神經元獨立演化，集體計算則通過明確的圖拓撲中的互動而產生。我們將TND實現為一個離散時間圖耦合動態系統，並在單人Pong的行為複製任務中進行案例研究評估。與Vanilla RNN、Sparse RNN、LSTM、封閉形式連續時間神經網絡（CfC）和Transformer基線相比，TND達到了最佳的捕獲率，每輪平均17.47次連續捕獲，超過最強基線的三倍以上。這些結果表明，從層級動態轉變為神經元動態為序列建模提供了一種有效的歸納偏差。

##### **Beyond Hooking Onto the World: Referential Profiles and the Numerical Structure of LLM Grounding**
2606.21195v1 by Joo Yull Rhee

This paper revisits the grounding problem for large language models in light of recent vector-grounding accounts. I accept the shift from classical symbol grounding to vector grounding, but argue that the current debate remains incomplete in two respects. First, reference is often treated too thinly, as if it were a fixed link between an isolated expression and an object. I argue instead that reference is profile-based, context-sensitive, discourse-level, affectively shaped, and norm-governed. Even in the human case, reference is publicly stabilized through patterns of use, correction, distinction, inference, and continuation rather than through identical private representations. Second, vector grounding requires an account of numerical realization. LLMs do not acquire reference through human perception, memory, intention, embodiment, or understanding. Rather, through optimization, they parameterize linguistic traces of human world-directed practice. In a finite vector system, referential profiles must be distributed, may be superposed, and are recovered through context-sensitive computation. Weights, activations, attention-mediated hidden states, softmax-trained contrasts, and inner-product alignments are the mathematical sites at which inherited linguistic relations become stable and causally active. Mechanistic interpretability findings, including entity-like features, knowledge neurons, and emotion-related activation directions, provide indirect support for this view. They do not show that LLMs possess human reference. They support a more limited thesis: LLMs may possess derivative, language-mediated, profile-based, and numerically structured forms of reference.

摘要：這篇論文重新檢視了大型語言模型的基礎問題，考慮到最近的向量基礎說法。<lb/>我接受從傳統符號基礎轉向向量基礎的變化，但我認為當前的辯論在兩個方面仍然不完整。<lb/>首先，參考通常被過於簡化地對待，就好像它是孤立表達與對象之間的固定連結。<lb/>我則主張參考是基於輪廓的、上下文敏感的、話語層面的、情感塑造的，並且受到規範約束。<lb/>即使在人的情況下，參考也是通過使用、修正、區分、推理和延續的模式來公開穩定，而不是通過相同的私人表徵。<lb/>其次，向量基礎需要對數字實現的解釋。<lb/>大型語言模型並不是通過人類的感知、記憶、意圖、具身性或理解來獲得參考。<lb/>相反，通過優化，它們對人類面向世界的實踐的語言痕跡進行參數化。<lb/>在有限的向量系統中，參考輪廓必須是分佈的，可以是重疊的，並且通過上下文敏感的計算來恢復。<lb/>權重、激活、注意力介導的隱藏狀態、softmax訓練的對比以及內積對齊是遺傳語言關係變得穩定和因果活躍的數學場域。<lb/>機械可解釋性研究結果，包括類似實體的特徵、知識神經元和情感相關的激活方向，為這一觀點提供了間接支持。<lb/>它們並未顯示大型語言模型擁有人類參考。<lb/>它們支持一個更有限的論點：大型語言模型可能擁有衍生的、語言介導的、基於輪廓的和數字結構化的參考形式。

##### **Context-Aware Generative AI for Automated Telecom Test Script Generation**
2606.21151v1 by Gautam Prasad, Chandramohan T. N., Joy Bose

Automated test generation for telecom software systems and networks has advanced significantly with the adoption of machine learning and rule-based approaches. However, most existing solutions generate static test suites against a snapshot of the system; as code, configurations, topologies, and key performance indicators (KPIs) evolve, these tests quickly become outdated or misaligned with the live system. There is currently no widely adopted solution that continuously detects fine-grained changes and selectively adapts only the affected tests without regenerating entire test suites. This paper presents a context-aware generative AI framework for automated telecom test script generation that treats testing as a continuously adapting process driven by the current state of the system rather than a static artifact. The central contribution is delta-conditioned test generation over a live knowledge graph: our approach employs a continuously updated knowledge graph (KG) as a single source of truth, a delta engine for fine-grained change detection, and a KG-guided generative AI agent, operating via the Model Context Protocol (MCP), to create, update, or retire test cases automatically. We further integrate Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) to enrich reasoning with telecom-domain knowledge and historical artifacts. We demonstrate applicability across software-system and telecom-network use cases, including a Python-based KPI monitoring application managed in GitLab, and show how the framework reduces manual effort, improves test relevance, and accelerates test cycles.

摘要：自動化測試生成在電信軟體系統和網路方面隨著機器學習和基於規則的方法的採用而顯著進步。<lb/>然而，大多數現有解決方案是針對系統快照生成靜態測試套件；隨著代碼、配置、拓撲和關鍵績效指標（KPI）的演變，這些測試很快就會過時或與實時系統不匹配。<lb/>目前尚無廣泛採用的解決方案能夠持續檢測細粒度變更，並僅選擇性地調整受影響的測試，而無需重新生成整個測試套件。<lb/>本文提出了一個上下文感知的生成式人工智慧框架，用於自動化電信測試腳本生成，將測試視為一個根據系統當前狀態持續適應的過程，而非靜態的產物。<lb/>其核心貢獻是基於實時知識圖的增量條件測試生成：我們的方法使用不斷更新的知識圖（KG）作為唯一的真實來源，並利用增量引擎進行細粒度變更檢測，以及通過模型上下文協議（MCP）運作的KG引導生成式AI代理，自動創建、更新或退役測試案例。<lb/>我們進一步整合檢索增強生成（RAG），以豐富電信領域知識和歷史文物的推理。<lb/>我們展示了該框架在軟體系統和電信網路用例中的適用性，包括在GitLab中管理的基於Python的KPI監控應用程式，並展示了該框架如何減少手動工作、提高測試相關性並加快測試週期。

##### **PulseCX: Breaking the Closed-World Assumption in Real-Time CX**
2606.21124v1 by Rajat Agarwal, Suvidha Tripathi, Shubham Sharma

Conversational AI agents in Customer Experience (CX) typically suffer from a Closed-World Constraint, ignoring high-velocity external shifts like viral trends or outages. Ad-hoc web search attempts to bridge this gap but often introduce prohibitive latency and context poisoning. We introduce PulseCX, a framework that decouples knowledge acquisition from consumption. Adopting a structure-first paradigm, PulseCX employs an asynchronous agent to linearize signals into a Decay-Aware Temporal Knowledge Graph (DA-TKG) governed by reinforcement--decay dynamics to actively manage information lifecycles. By coupling this self-evolving memory with hierarchical intent gating, PulseCX removes synchronous search bottlenecks (<10ms overhead) and drives significant gains in Intent Resolution (IRR) and Customer Satisfaction (s-CSAT) in dynamic environments.

摘要：對話式人工智慧代理在客戶體驗 (CX) 中通常受到封閉世界限制的影響，忽略了像病毒趨勢或故障這樣的高速度外部變化。臨時的網路搜尋試圖彌補這一差距，但往往會引入過高的延遲和上下文污染。我們介紹了 PulseCX，一個將知識獲取與消費解耦的框架。採用結構優先的範式，PulseCX 使用異步代理將信號線性化為一個受強化-衰減動力學驅動的衰減感知時間知識圖 (DA-TKG)，以主動管理信息生命周期。通過將這種自我演化的記憶與分層意圖閘結合，PulseCX 消除了同步搜尋瓶頸（<10ms 的開銷），並在動態環境中驅動意圖解析 (IRR) 和客戶滿意度 (s-CSAT) 的顯著提升。

##### **A Multi-Agent Audit Framework for High-Stakes Reasoning: Evaluation and Interpretability in Clinical Mental Health Screening**
2606.21123v1 by Jingchen Ye, Yanpei Yu, Luyao Zhang

High-stakes reasoning tasks necessitate transparent and verifiable workflows, yet conventional single-model large language models (LLMs) often struggle with hallucination and low interpretability under zero-shot paradigms. To address this general AI challenge, we propose a Multi-Agent Audit Framework that simulates a collaborative, multi-step verification process. We empirically validate this architecture in the sensitive domain of clinical mental health screening using a modular LangChain workflow. Our framework decomposes the reasoning process into a Perception Agent, Knowledge Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG), Chain-of-Thought (CoT) clinical inference, and a critical Audit verification stage.
