摘要：這篇論文探索了一種新穎的腦部解碼模型，用於通過雙通路架構來感知三維形狀，該架構模仿生物視覺。我們的生物啟發方法實現了針對物體身份和空間方向的獨立解碼模塊，靈感來自於腹側和背側通路，並在連續旋轉過程中進行。 我們採用圓形回歸進行角度預測，並開發了基於腦電圖的多視角擴散技術以進行三維重建。我們的方法成功地從腦電圖信號中解碼物體身份和空間方向，並能夠從神經活動中進行三維重建，解釋性分析顯示腹側、背側和運動相關通道的時間結構參與，而不是靜態的腹側主導支持物體和角度解碼。

##### **The Score Granularity Gap in Black-Box LLM Classification: A Comparative Study of Confidence Constructions**
2606.22179v1 by Ao Sun, Tian Sun, Jiaxing Geng

Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as black-box classifiers in pipelines that automate confident decisions and route uncertain ones to human review. Such selective prediction needs a confidence score that an operator can threshold at a chosen risk level. Prior work asks whether LLM confidence is well calibrated or well ranked; we ask a complementary, deployment-oriented question that has been largely overlooked: at what resolution can the score be thresholded? We call the answer the score granularity gap. Through a controlled comparison of seven ways to build a confidence score, from a single verbalized number, to token probabilities, to querying the model many times and combining the answers, across 25 model-dataset pairs (9 LLMs, 3 benchmarks), we find that single-shot verbalized confidence, once correctly converted to a class probability, ranks cases surprisingly well, yet takes only a handful of distinct values. It therefore offers an operator only a few coarse thresholds, no matter how well it ranks. We show which constructions widen this gap, at what inference cost, and with what effect on ranking, notably that multi-query aggregation helps weak models but can degrade already-strong ones. We translate these trade-offs into concrete deployment guidance.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越多地被用作黑箱分類器，在自動化自信決策的流程中，並將不確定的決策交由人類審核。這種選擇性預測需要一個信心分數，操作員可以在選定的風險水平上進行閾值設定。先前的研究詢問LLM的信心是否經過良好校準或良好排序；我們提出了一個互補的、以部署為導向的問題，這個問題在很大程度上被忽視：這個分數可以在什麼解析度下進行閾值設定？我們將這個答案稱為分數粒度差距。通過對七種構建信心分數的方法進行控制比較，從單一的口頭數字到標記概率，再到多次查詢模型並結合答案，涵蓋25個模型-數據集對（9個LLMs，3個基準），我們發現單次口頭表達的信心，一旦正確轉換為類別概率，對案例的排序意外地良好，但僅取幾個不同的值。因此，無論其排序效果多麼良好，它僅為操作員提供了幾個粗略的閾值。我們展示了哪些構造擴大了這一差距，推理成本是多少，以及對排序的影響，特別是多查詢聚合有助於弱模型，但可能會降低已經強大的模型的表現。我們將這些權衡轉化為具體的部署指導。

##### **DSSCNet: A Transfer Learning Framework for Cross-Corpus Dysarthric Speech Severity Classification**
2606.22178v1 by Arnab Kumar Roy, Hemant Kumar Kathania, Paban Sapkota, Sudarsana Reddy Kadiri, Shrikanth Narayanan

Dysarthric speech severity classification is challenging due to speaker variability, class imbalance, and limited datasets. This study introduces DSSCNet, a deep learning model that employs transfer learning and multi-corpus learning to enhance speaker-independent classification. By pre-training on one dysarthric speech corpus and fine-tuning on another, DSSCNet achieves improved feature extraction and cross-corpus generalization. Experimental results demonstrate that DSSCNet outperforms state-of-the-art models for speaker-independent severity classification, achieving 75.80\% accuracy on TORGO and 68.25\% on UA-Speech, significantly reducing misclassification errors. The findings confirm that leveraging knowledge transfer between datasets improves model robustness, making DSSCNet well-suited for automated dysarthria assessment. This research contributes to the development of more effective assistive speech technologies for individuals with speech impairments.

摘要：語音障礙的語音嚴重程度分類因講者變異性、類別不平衡和有限的數據集而具有挑戰性。這項研究介紹了DSSCNet，一種深度學習模型，利用轉移學習和多語料庫學習來增強與講者無關的分類。通過在一個語音障礙語音語料庫上進行預訓練，並在另一個語料庫上進行微調，DSSCNet實現了改進的特徵提取和跨語料庫的泛化。實驗結果顯示，DSSCNet在與講者無關的嚴重程度分類中超越了最先進的模型，在TORGO上達到75.80\%的準確率，在UA-Speech上達到68.25\%，顯著減少了錯誤分類的次數。研究結果確認了在數據集之間利用知識轉移可以提高模型的穩健性，使DSSCNet非常適合自動化的語音障礙評估。這項研究有助於開發更有效的輔助語音技術，幫助有語音障礙的人士。

##### **How Well Do Self-Supervised Speech Models Encode Age and Gender in Children's Speech? A Layer-Wise Analysis Across Multiple Architectures**
2606.22177v1 by Abhijit Sinha, Hemant Kumar Kathania, Mohit Joshi, Harishankar Kumar, Shrikanth Narayanan, Sudarsana Reddy Kadiri

Self-supervised learning (SSL) models have become a central component of modern speech processing systems, as they enable the learning of rich acoustic representations without reliance on labeled data. Despite their success on adult speech, it remains unclear how effectively these models capture speaker-related attributes such as age and gender in children's speech, which differs substantially from adult speech due to ongoing physiological and cognitive development. Higher pitch, increased articulatory variability, and age-dependent acoustic changes make children's speech a particularly challenging domain. In this work, we present a comprehensive analysis of how age and gender information is encoded across layers of four widely used SSL models: Wav2Vec2, HuBERT, Data2Vec, and WavLM. Layer-wise features are extracted and evaluated using a lightweight CNN on two benchmark children's speech corpora, PFSTAR and CMU Kids. To analyze feature compactness and redundancy, PCA is applied to identify redundancy and highlight the dimensions that contribute most to classification performance. Experimental results show that age- and gender-related information is unevenly distributed across SSL layers, with early to mid-level layers encoding the strongest paralinguistic cues. HuBERT achieves the best overall performance for age classification, while Wav2Vec2 and HuBERT lead gender classification on PFSTAR and CMU Kids, respectively. Beyond single-split evaluation, we further demonstrate that these findings remain stable under speaker-wise cross-validation, layer aggregation, and cross-database evaluation, indicating robustness to data imbalance and domain mismatch. Finally, we show that reliable age and gender classification is achievable even from short speech segments of 1--3 seconds.

摘要：自我監督學習（SSL）模型已成為現代語音處理系統的核心組成部分，因為它們能夠在不依賴標記數據的情況下學習豐富的聲學表示。儘管這些模型在成人語音上的成功，但尚不清楚這些模型在捕捉兒童語音中與說話者相關的屬性（如年齡和性別）方面的有效性，因為兒童語音因持續的生理和認知發展而與成人語音有顯著不同。較高的音調、增加的發音變異性以及年齡依賴的聲學變化使得兒童語音成為一個特別具有挑戰性的領域。在這項工作中，我們對四個廣泛使用的SSL模型（Wav2Vec2、HuBERT、Data2Vec和WavLM）中年齡和性別信息如何在各層中編碼進行了全面分析。我們提取並評估層級特徵，使用輕量級CNN在兩個基準兒童語音語料庫PFSTAR和CMU Kids上進行評估。為了分析特徵的緊湊性和冗餘性，我們應用PCA來識別冗餘並突出對分類性能貢獻最大的維度。實驗結果顯示，與年齡和性別相關的信息在SSL層中分佈不均，早期到中層編碼了最強的副語言線索。HuBERT在年齡分類方面達到了最佳的整體性能，而Wav2Vec2和HuBERT在PFSTAR和CMU Kids上分別領導性別分類。除了單一切分評估外，我們進一步證明這些發現即使在說話者交叉驗證、層級聚合和跨數據庫評估下仍然穩定，顯示出對數據不平衡和領域不匹配的魯棒性。最後，我們顯示即使從1到3秒的短語音片段中也能實現可靠的年齡和性別分類。

##### **Rebuttals Move Peer-Review Scores, but Initial-Review Structure Bounds the Movement**
2606.22166v1 by Mathieu Louis, Tibo Vanleke, Vincent Ginis, Andres Algaba

Author rebuttals are the main post-submission window in peer review, but their effect on reviewer scores remains hard to measure because score updates mix rebuttal content with initial score position, paper-level consensus, reviewer confidence, and discussion dynamics. We study ICLR 2024-2025 using 73,000 reviewer trajectories with externally archived pre- and post-rebuttal scores, and use LLMs only as measurement instruments. Gemini Flash 3.0 predicts implied pre-rebuttal scores from score-stripped review text. The resulting text-score offset predicts later movement, with score-increase rates rising from 8.3% when text reads below the assigned score to 31.9% when it reads above. Claude Opus 4.6 induces, and outcome-blinded Gemini Flash 3.0 validates, a 44-feature taxonomy of resolved reviewer-author exchanges, where 23 features replicate across model and held-out year under Bonferroni correction. In the rebuttal-engaged benchmark (n=6,705), initial-review structure already predicts much score movement (AUC=0.747, minimal AUC=0.696), while adding the resolved exchange raises AUC to 0.804. Rebuttals can move scores, but measurable movement is bounded by initial-review structure, and robust exchange signals are mostly rebuttal failure modes.

摘要：作者的反駁是同行評審中提交後的主要窗口，但其對評審分數的影響仍然難以衡量，因為分數更新將反駁內容與初始分數位置、論文層級共識、評審信心和討論動態混合在一起。我們使用73,000條評審軌跡研究ICLR 2024-2025，這些軌跡包含外部存檔的反駁前後分數，並僅將LLMs用作測量工具。Gemini Flash 3.0從去除分數的評審文本中預測隱含的反駁前分數。由此產生的文本-分數偏移預測後續的變動，當文本讀取低於分配分數時，分數增加率為8.3%，而當其讀取高於分配分數時，則上升至31.9%。Claude Opus 4.6引發，且結果盲化的Gemini Flash 3.0驗證了一個包含44個特徵的解決評審-作者交流的分類法，其中23個特徵在模型和保留年份中在Bonferroni修正下複製。在參與反駁的基準中（n=6,705），初始評審結構已經預測了大量的分數變動（AUC=0.747，最小AUC=0.696），而添加解決的交流則將AUC提高至0.804。反駁可以改變分數，但可衡量的變動受限於初始評審結構，而穩健的交流信號主要是反駁失敗模式。

##### **$π$-RAG: Oblivious Retrieval via Semantic Quantization and Transcendental Addressing for Large Language Models**
2606.22153v1 by Aniket Wattamwar, Mrunal Kakirwar

This paper introduces $π$-RAG, a novel architecture for oblivious retrieval that decouples Large Language Models (LLMs) from sensitive data storage without sacrificing semantic understanding. Traditional Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) architectures expose raw vector embeddings to potential inversion attacks and nondeterministic retrieval failures. To address this, we utilize the digits of $π$ as a source of transcendental entropy, creating an immutable indirection layer between the LLM and private records. The value $π$ provides immutability, is uneditable and math governs it. The architecture also introduces a Semantic Quantization Layer. This layer projects user inputs onto a pre-computed manifold of Canonical Intent Centroids. RAG performs vector cosine similarity but here it maps the centroids to deterministic offsets via cryptographic salt. The resulting $π$-key is a pointer to standardized payload from the actual datastore. By replacing direct access to the datastore via LLM with this transcendental layer, $π$-RAG mathematically guarantees that the inference remains oblivious to the data. This architecture unifies deterministic randomness, auditability, and differential privacy, demonstrating high efficacy for high-compliance sectors such as finance and healthcare.

摘要：這篇論文介紹了 $π$-RAG，一種新穎的無知檢索架構，將大型語言模型（LLMs）與敏感數據存儲解耦，而不犧牲語義理解。傳統的檢索增強生成（RAG）架構將原始向量嵌入暴露於潛在的反演攻擊和非確定性檢索失敗。為了解決這個問題，我們利用 $π$ 的數字作為超越熵的來源，創建了一個不變的間接層，將 LLM 與私有記錄隔開。值 $π$ 提供不變性，無法編輯，且由數學所支配。該架構還引入了一個語義量化層。這一層將用戶輸入投影到預計算的典範意圖重心流形上。RAG 執行向量餘弦相似度，但在這裡它通過加密鹽將重心映射到確定性偏移量。生成的 $π$-鍵是一個指向實際數據存儲中標準化有效負載的指針。通過用這個超越層替代 LLM 對數據存儲的直接訪問，$π$-RAG 在數學上保證推理對數據保持無知。該架構統一了確定性隨機性、可審計性和差異隱私，顯示出對於高合規性行業如金融和醫療保健的高效性。

##### **SAGE: An Expert-Annotated South Asian GI Endoscopy Dataset for Multimodal Learning and Hallucination Analysis**
2606.22144v1 by Niyoj Oli, Sachin Acharya, Sandesh Pokhrel, Sanjay Bhandari, Ramesh Rana, Nikesh Mani Shrestha, Ram Bahadur Gurung, Yash Raj Shrestha, Prashnna K Gyawali, Binod Bhattarai

Gastrointestinal cancers represent a growing health burden in the South Asian region, driven largely by rapid changes in socio-economic conditions & lifestyle habits. However, early diagnosis of such malignancies remains a significant challenge, largely due to a lack of modern equipment, lack of financial support, and a scarcity of GI experts. AI-assisted diagnosis & report generation, show great promise in alleviating this problem by providing low-skill manpower the technical expertise to perform diagnosis. However, almost all open-source, publicly available datasets are predominantly collected from the European region, with no representation from the South Asian region. The lack of open-source GI datasets from diverse geographic regions has made it difficult to assess whether population bias is present in existing models, and to develop geographically inclusive AI tools for automated GI diagnosis. To address this gap, we introduce SAGE: An Expert-Annotated South Asian GI Endoscopy dataset for image captioning, multi-label classification, and visual question answering (VQA) tasks. It consists of 1,300 images, their captions along with hallucination tag, 18 labels and 14,726 question-answer pairs making it well-suited for diverse range of tasks including classification, benchmarking, and fine-tuning large multimodal models (LMMs). We further conducted benchmarking of multi-class classifiers on the effect of population shift in GI imaging AI tasks, and contemporary LMMs on their performance. Our study reveals that task-specific models, such as multi-class classification models, suffer the most, with an average performance drop of 58% when evaluated on the South Asian dataset. For contemporary LMMs, benchmarking reveals a substantial drop in the average GREEN score for anatomical landmark detection (0.308) and abnormality detection (0.410).

摘要：腸胃道癌症在南亞地區代表著日益增長的健康負擔，這主要是由於社會經濟條件和生活習慣的快速變化。然而，這類惡性腫瘤的早期診斷仍然是一個重大挑戰，主要是由於缺乏現代設備、缺乏財政支持以及腸胃專家的稀缺。人工智慧輔助的診斷和報告生成在緩解這一問題方面顯示出巨大的潛力，通過為低技能人力提供技術專業知識來進行診斷。然而，幾乎所有公開的開源數據集主要來自歐洲地區，南亞地區則沒有代表性。來自不同地理區域的開源腸胃數據集的缺乏使得評估現有模型中是否存在人口偏見變得困難，並且難以開發地理包容性的自動化腸胃診斷人工智慧工具。為了解決這一空白，我們介紹了SAGE：一個專家註釋的南亞腸胃內鏡數據集，用於圖像標題生成、多標籤分類和視覺問題回答（VQA）任務。該數據集包含1,300張圖像、它們的標題及其幻覺標籤、18個標籤和14,726個問答對，使其非常適合包括分類、基準測試和微調大型多模態模型（LMMs）在內的各種任務。我們進一步對多類別分類器在腸胃影像人工智慧任務中的人口變遷影響及當代LMM的性能進行了基準測試。我們的研究顯示，特定任務模型，如多類別分類模型，受到的影響最大，在南亞數據集上評估時平均性能下降58%。對於當代LMM，基準測試顯示解剖標誌檢測（0.308）和異常檢測（0.410）的平均GREEN分數顯著下降。

##### **BioMatrix: Towards a Comprehensive Biological Foundation Model Spanning the Modality Matrix of Sequences, Structures, and Language**
2606.22138v1 by Qizhi Pei, Zhimeng Zhou, Yi Duan, Yiyang Zhao, Wei Li, Han Guo, Liang He, Chengping Li, Chang-Yu Hsieh, Conghui He, Rui Yan, Lijun Wu

We present BioMatrix, the first multimodal foundation model that natively integrates sequences, structures, and natural language for both molecules and proteins within a single decoder-only architecture. Existing biological foundation models pursue native multimodality and broad entity coverage separately: those that fuse multiple modalities under a shared objective remain confined to a single entity type, while those spanning multiple entity types either omit explicit structural modeling or rely on adapter-based designs in which the model cannot natively generate the very modalities it can read. BioMatrix closes this gap by mapping molecular sequences (supporting both SMILES and SELFIES notations), molecular structures, protein sequences, protein structures, and natural language into a shared discrete token space through a unified tokenization scheme, so that all modalities are consumed and produced uniformly under a single next-token prediction objective -- without external encoders, projection adapters, or modality-specific output heads. Built upon the Qwen3 language model (1.7B and 4B), BioMatrix is continually pretrained on 304.4 billion tokens spanning general and domain-specific text, sequence and structure views of molecules and proteins, and cross-modal corpora that interleave biomolecular entities with scientific text and link distinct entities through molecule-protein and protein-protein interaction data. After tuning on a comprehensive suite of downstream applications covering 80 tasks across 6 categories -- encompassing single-entity and multi-entity understanding and generation tasks across and within modalities -- BioMatrix achieves state-of-the-art or competitive performance on 77 out of 80 tasks, demonstrating that a single, natively multimodal generalist model can effectively match or surpass specialized approaches across a wide range of biological tasks.

摘要：我們介紹 BioMatrix，首個原生整合分子和蛋白質的序列、結構和自然語言的多模態基礎模型，採用單一解碼器架構。現有的生物基礎模型分別追求原生多模態和廣泛的實體覆蓋：那些在共享目標下融合多種模態的模型仍然限制於單一實體類型，而那些跨越多種實體類型的模型則要麼省略明確的結構建模，要麼依賴於適配器設計，這使得模型無法原生生成它能夠讀取的模態。BioMatrix 通過將分子序列（支持 SMILES 和 SELFIES 表示法）、分子結構、蛋白質序列、蛋白質結構和自然語言映射到共享的離散標記空間，通過統一的標記化方案，填補了這一空白，使所有模態在單一的下一標記預測目標下被統一消耗和生成——無需外部編碼器、投影適配器或特定模態的輸出頭。BioMatrix 基於 Qwen3 語言模型（1.7B 和 4B），持續在 3044 億個標記上進行預訓練，涵蓋一般和領域特定的文本、分子和蛋白質的序列和結構視圖，以及交錯生物分子實體與科學文本的跨模態語料庫，並通過分子-蛋白質和蛋白質-蛋白質互動數據鏈接不同實體。在針對涵蓋 80 個任務的綜合下游應用進行調整後——包括跨模態和內部模態的單一實體和多實體理解及生成任務——BioMatrix 在 80 個任務中的 77 個上達到了最先進或具競爭力的性能，證明了一個單一的、原生多模態的通用模型能有效匹配或超越在廣泛生物任務上的專門方法。

##### **From Recognition to Understanding: Unlocking Cognitive Time Series Reasoning with LLMs**
2606.22126v1 by Xin Qiu, Junlong Tong, Yao Zhang, Yunpu Ma, Wei Zhang, Xiaoyu Shen

Time series analysis has recently been coupled with Large Language Models (LLMs) to leverage their reasoning and world knowledge capabilities, yet gains remain limited. We attribute this to a fundamental mismatch between existing task formulations and LLM strengths: most settings reduce time series understanding to curve-fitting systems, focusing on low-level prediction while ignoring the semantic, contextual, and reasoning-intensive nature of real-world temporal decision-making.To address these limitations, we introduce TSCognition, a multimodal benchmark for multi-dimensional time series reasoning. It collects real-world time series and textual information from 15 public sources and constructs approximately 41K QA samples around five cognitive reasoning tasks: Decoding, Grounding, Inferring, Extrapolating, and Acting. Building on this, we further propose TSAlign, a unified framework that encodes time series into compact patch-level representations and aligns them with semantic directions in the LLM embedding space via gated residual injection and multivariate fusion.Experiments show that TSAlign outperforms existing LLM, VLM, and time series QA baselines on TSCognition and the publicly available TimerBed benchmark while substantially reducing computational cost.Code is available at: [https://github.com/EIT-NLP/CognitiveTSR](https://github.com/EIT-NLP/CognitiveTSR)

摘要：時間序列分析最近與大型語言模型（LLMs）結合，以利用其推理和世界知識能力，但收益仍然有限。我們將此歸因於現有任務表述與LLM優勢之間的根本不匹配：大多數設置將時間序列理解簡化為曲線擬合系統，專注於低層次的預測，同時忽略了現實世界時間決策的語義、上下文和推理密集性質。為了解決這些限制，我們介紹了TSCognition，一個多模態基準，用於多維時間序列推理。它從15個公共來源收集現實世界的時間序列和文本信息，並圍繞五個認知推理任務構建約41K的問答樣本：解碼、基礎、推斷、外推和行動。在此基礎上，我們進一步提出了TSAlign，一個統一框架，將時間序列編碼為緊湊的補丁級表示，並通過門控殘差注入和多變量融合將其與LLM嵌入空間中的語義方向對齊。實驗表明，TSAlign在TSCognition和公開可用的TimerBed基準上超越了現有的LLM、VLM和時間序列問答基準，同時顯著降低了計算成本。代碼可在以下網址獲得：[https://github.com/EIT-NLP/CognitiveTSR](https://github.com/EIT-NLP/CognitiveTSR)

##### **KITE: Decoupling Kinematics and Interaction for Zero-Shot Cross-Embodiment Manipulation**
2606.22113v1 by Qianxu Wang, Kuan Fang

Generalizing manipulation policies across robot embodiments remains difficult because standard policies entangle task reasoning with embodiment-specific motor control. We study zero-shot cross-embodiment manipulation, where a policy trained on source embodiments must be deployed on a structurally different target embodiment without additional task demonstrations. We introduce Kinematic Interaction Transfer across Embodiments (KITE), which decouples manipulation into embodiment-agnostic task reasoning and embodiment-specific motor control, connected through a learned latent representation of interaction intent based on contact patterns. Task reasoning is performed by a shared policy that predicts latent intents from source demonstrations, while motor control is performed by an intent-conditioned action decoder learned from each embodiment's kinematic model. With KITE, adaptation to a new embodiment requires only training a new action decoder using its kinematic model, without recollecting demonstration data. We evaluate KITE on three manipulation tasks spanning transfer between parallel grippers, dexterous hands, and composite embodiments. KITE consistently achieves zero-shot transfer to structurally different target embodiments, outperforming state-of-the-art baselines in transfer success and task-embodiment scope.

摘要：一般化機器人實體之間的操作策略仍然困難，因為標準策略將任務推理與特定實體的運動控制糾纏在一起。<lb/>我們研究零樣本跨實體操作，其中在源實體上訓練的策略必須在結構上不同的目標實體上部署，而無需額外的任務演示。<lb/>我們引入了跨實體的運動互動轉移（Kinematic Interaction Transfer across Embodiments，KITE），它將操作解耦為與實體無關的任務推理和特定實體的運動控制，通過基於接觸模式的互動意圖的學習潛在表示相連接。<lb/>任務推理由共享策略執行，該策略從源演示中預測潛在意圖，而運動控制則由從每個實體的運動模型學習的意圖條件動作解碼器執行。<lb/>使用KITE，適應新實體只需使用其運動模型訓練新的動作解碼器，而無需重新收集演示數據。<lb/>我們在三個操作任務上評估KITE，這些任務涵蓋了平行夾爪、靈巧手和複合實體之間的轉移。<lb/>KITE始終實現對結構上不同的目標實體的零樣本轉移，在轉移成功率和任務-實體範圍方面超越了最先進的基準。

##### **TraceView: Interactive Visualization of Agentic Program Repair Trajectories**
2606.22110v1 by Amirali Sajadi, Tu Nguyen, Kimmie Huynh, Esteban Parra, Preetha Chatterjee

LLM-based automated program repair (APR) agents generate patches to fix software bugs with minimal human intervention. These agents often produce long trajectories of reasoning, tool use, and feedback to produce candidate patches. Final patch outcomes show whether a repair attempt succeeded or failed, but they do not show how the agent reached that outcome, or where the process became repetitive or misaligned with the task. This makes agentic repair failures difficult to diagnose, reproduce, and prevent. To help developers address these challenges, we present TraceView, an interactive tool for labeling and visualizing repair trajectories from APR systems. TraceView organizes raw and pre-labeled agentic runs with Thought, Action, and Result components to support semantic relation labeling and diagnosis, and renders the resulting trajectory as graph views. Furthermore, TraceView provides relation filters, patch outcome summaries, metrics, and node-level evidence panels to help users inspect how reasoning, actions, and feedback connect across the various steps of an agentic repair attempt. We evaluate TraceView with five researchers through a survey-based user study. Participants reported that TraceView made trajectories easier to scan and that its overview-to-detail workflow helped them better understand repair behavior. The TraceView source code is available at https://github.com/SOAR-Lab/agent-traj-visualization. A screencast of TraceView is available at https://youtu.be/9ZCh7Ifj2AQ.

摘要：LLM 基於的自動程式修復 (APR) 代理生成修補程式以修復軟體錯誤，並且需要最少的人為干預。這些代理通常產生長時間的推理、工具使用和反饋，以生成候選修補程式。最終的修補結果顯示修復嘗試是成功還是失敗，但它們並不顯示代理如何達到該結果，或過程中何時變得重複或與任務不一致。這使得代理修復失敗難以診斷、重現和預防。為了幫助開發者解決這些挑戰，我們提出了 TraceView，一個用於標記和可視化 APR 系統修復軌跡的互動工具。TraceView 組織原始和預標記的代理運行，包含思考、行動和結果組件，以支持語義關係標記和診斷，並將結果軌跡呈現為圖形視圖。此外，TraceView 還提供關係過濾器、修補結果摘要、指標和節點級證據面板，以幫助用戶檢查推理、行動和反饋如何在代理修復嘗試的各個步驟中相互連接。我們通過基於調查的用戶研究，與五位研究人員評估了 TraceView。參與者報告說，TraceView 使軌跡更容易掃描，並且其概覽到詳細的工作流程幫助他們更好地理解修復行為。TraceView 的源代碼可在 https://github.com/SOAR-Lab/agent-traj-visualization 獲得。TraceView 的螢幕錄像可在 https://youtu.be/9ZCh7Ifj2AQ 獲得。

##### **Plurification in/of language technology -- The integration of culture in next-generation AI**
2606.22097v1 by Gertraud Koch, Fausto Giunchiglia

The paper explores how "culture" can be operationalised in Natural Language Processing (NLP) and what this reveals about the possibilities and limits of considering a plurality of cultural backgrounds in technological design. It proposes that cultural alignment cannot be achieved only by adding more examples of "other cultures", rather it requires plural epistemologies: allowing multiple, locally grounded ways of knowing. To analyze how this plurality of knowing can be addressed in NLP, the paper uses a socio-technical model of language technology (LT) design, the five layers of technological activity model, for collecting and systematizing approaches to culture in NLP. The analysis shows that while NLP research has made progress toward more culturally sensitive systems, many approaches remain partial, addressing "culture" primarily at the level of output or representation while leaving deeper questions of power, governance, and social context unresolved. The paper concludes that operationalising culture requires much more than technical adaptation; it suggests a reflexive and plural socio-technical approach that navigates potentials and limits of computational formalisation for accounting multiple linguistic and socio-cultural backgrounds.

摘要：這篇論文探討了如何在自然語言處理 (NLP) 中操作「文化」，以及這對於考慮多元文化背景在技術設計中的可能性和限制所揭示的內容。<lb/>它提出，文化對齊不僅僅是通過增加更多「其他文化」的例子來實現的，而是需要多元的認識論：允許多種本地化的認知方式。<lb/>為了分析如何在 NLP 中處理這種認知的多元性，該論文使用了語言技術 (LT) 設計的社會技術模型，即五層技術活動模型，以收集和系統化在 NLP 中對文化的不同方法。<lb/>分析顯示，儘管 NLP 研究在朝著更具文化敏感性的系統方面取得了進展，但許多方法仍然是片面的，主要在輸出或表徵層面上處理「文化」，而未能解決權力、治理和社會背景等更深層次的問題。<lb/>該論文總結道，操作文化需要的不僅僅是技術適應；它建議採用一種反思性和多元的社會技術方法，以應對計算形式化在考慮多種語言和社會文化背景方面的潛力和限制。

##### **Can Reasoning Models Detect Changes to their Chains of Thought?**
2606.22085v1 by Sathvik Napa, Utkarsh Singh, Chengyuan Xue, Miriam Wanner, William Walden

There are many reasons one may want to edit a model's chain of thought (CoT) -- e.g., to prefill it with reasoning from a stronger model or to remove steps that may yield unsafe outputs. The success of these interventions plausibly depends on a model's inability to notice them, as the model may alter its behavior if it suspects tampering. In this work, we study whether recent reasoning models are able to detect such interventions on their CoTs under a variety of conditions: both during reasoning and after it, and when prefilled both with their own CoTs and with those of other models. Broadly, we find that (i) models exhibit only very modest detection accuracy; (ii) models struggle to identify *how* their CoT was modified; and (iii) models are about as good at detecting changes to their own CoTs as to those of other models.

摘要：有許多原因可能使人們想要編輯模型的思考鏈（CoT）——例如，將其預填充為來自更強模型的推理，或移除可能產生不安全輸出的步驟。這些干預的成功可能取決於模型是否無法察覺到它們，因為如果模型懷疑被篡改，它可能會改變其行為。在這項工作中，我們研究最近的推理模型是否能在各種條件下檢測到其CoT上的這些干預：無論是在推理過程中還是在推理之後，以及在預填充自己CoT和其他模型的CoT時。總體而言，我們發現（i）模型的檢測準確性僅非常有限；（ii）模型難以識別*如何*修改其CoT；以及（iii）模型檢測自己CoT的變更和其他模型CoT的變更的能力大致相當。

##### **CodeTeam: An LLM-Powered Multi-Agent Framework for Repository-Level Code Generation**
2606.22082v1 by Yifei Wang, Ruiyin Li, Peng Liang, Qiong Feng, Zengyang Li, Mojtaba Shahin, Arif Ali Khan

Natural language to repository generation (NL2Repo) requires a system to construct an entire software repository from a natural-language requirements document. Compared with function-level code generation, this task demands longer planning horizons, stable interfaces across files, and iterative debugging of cross-file inconsistencies. To address these challenges, we propose CodeTeam, an LLM-based multi-agent framework that separates planning, decision making, and implementation into distinct, coordinated stages. In the planning stage, multiple Architect agents draft competing software design sketches (SDS), optionally grounded by retrieved design references. A CTO agent then evaluates, selects, and normalizes the most promising SDS into a machine-checkable contract that specifies file ownership, public interfaces, and dependency constraints. In the implementation stage, Developer agents generate code under a dependency-aware scheduler with bounded context and lightweight Git-based coordination, while a QA agent runs tests and drives iterative repairs. On the synthesis-based SketchEval benchmark, we explicitly compare CodeTeam's prompt-engineering (PE) and supervised fine-tuning (SFT) variants with the corresponding CodeS variants, where CodeTeam improves the overall SketchBLEU by 4.1 and 2.9 absolute points, respectively. On the execution-based NL2Repo-Bench benchmark, used as an external validation protocol, CodeTeam achieves the highest average test pass rate in both settings (34.6% PE, 42.3% SFT), confirming that the sketch-improvements extend to functional correctness under upstream test suites. Ablation results show that project-specific developer allocation and retrieval-augmented planning each contribute substantially to the SketchBLEU improvement (9.9% and 8.1% relative, respectively). CodeTeam and the experimental results are available at https://github.com/WhitenWhiten/CodeTeam

摘要：自然語言到倉庫生成（NL2Repo）需要一個系統來從自然語言需求文檔構建整個軟體倉庫。與功能級別的代碼生成相比，這項任務需要更長的規劃時間、更穩定的跨文件介面，以及對跨文件不一致性的迭代調試。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了CodeTeam，一個基於LLM的多代理框架，將規劃、決策和實施分為不同的協調階段。在規劃階段，多個架構代理草擬競爭性的軟體設計草圖（SDS），可選擇性地以檢索到的設計參考為基礎。然後，CTO代理評估、選擇並標準化最有前景的SDS，形成一個可機器檢查的合約，該合約指定文件所有權、公共介面和依賴約束。在實施階段，開發者代理在一個依賴感知的調度器下生成代碼，該調度器具有有限的上下文和輕量級的基於Git的協調，而QA代理則運行測試並推動迭代修復。在基於合成的SketchEval基準上，我們明確比較了CodeTeam的提示工程（PE）和監督微調（SFT）變體與相應的CodeS變體，其中CodeTeam的整體SketchBLEU分別提高了4.1和2.9個絕對點。在基於執行的NL2Repo-Bench基準上，作為外部驗證協議，CodeTeam在兩種設置中均達到了最高的平均測試通過率（34.6% PE，42.3% SFT），確認草圖改進延伸至上游測試套件下的功能正確性。消融結果顯示，專案特定的開發者分配和增強檢索的規劃各自對SketchBLEU的改善貢獻顯著（相對分別為9.9%和8.1%）。CodeTeam及其實驗結果可在https://github.com/WhitenWhiten/CodeTeam獲得。

##### **Where Does the Signal Live? A Web Data Recipe for Medical Encoder Pretraining**
2606.22079v1 by Bofeng Huang, Jacques Sun, Diane Bouchacourt, Nicolas Barascud, Fajwel Fogel

Web data curation has been widely studied for decoder Large Language Model (LLM) pretraining. Encoders for dense-terminology domains such as medicine, by contrast, are pretrained on small, manually-curated corpora that limit scalability and writing style diversity, a bottleneck even more severe in non-English clinical settings. Whether web-scale data curation also benefits encoder Masked Language Modeling (MLM) in a dense-terminology domain remains an open question. To address this, we introduce two complementary levers. Medical-term density filtering selects documents rich in medical terms. Signal-amplifying rephrasing uses an LLM to rewrite documents into denser variants with broader entity contexts. We instantiate the recipe on French medical NLP. The medical-term density filter outperforms the widely-used educational quality filter on downstream medical tasks, and the two complement each other. Signal-amplifying rephrasing alone improves on raw web data, and mixing it with filtered web data produces the largest gain. The recipe yields FineMed, a French medical pretraining corpus, and DoctoBERT, a state-of-the-art French medical encoder family evaluated on both the public benchmark DrBenchmark and a proprietary clinical Named Entity Recognition (NER) task.

摘要：網路數據策展已被廣泛研究以用於解碼器大型語言模型（LLM）的預訓練。相比之下，針對密集術語領域（如醫學）的編碼器則是在小型、手動策展的語料庫上進行預訓練，這限制了可擴展性和寫作風格的多樣性，這在非英語臨床環境中更是嚴重的瓶頸。網路規模的數據策展是否也能使密集術語領域的編碼器掩蔽語言模型（MLM）受益仍然是一個未解的問題。為了解決這個問題，我們引入了兩個互補的手段。醫學術語密度過濾器選擇富含醫學術語的文檔。信號增強重述使用LLM將文檔改寫成更密集的變體，並具有更廣泛的實體上下文。我們在法語醫學自然語言處理中實現了這個配方。醫學術語密度過濾器在下游醫學任務中表現優於廣泛使用的教育質量過濾器，且兩者互為補充。僅信號增強重述就改善了原始網路數據，並且將其與過濾後的網路數據混合會產生最大的增益。這個配方產生了FineMed，一個法語醫學預訓練語料庫，以及DoctoBERT，一個在公共基準DrBenchmark和專有臨床命名實體識別（NER）任務上評估的最先進法語醫學編碼器系列。

##### **New Smooth Loss functions for Robust Regression that Closely Approximate Absolute Error and Provide Improved Performance on Datasets With Significant Outliers**
2606.22068v1 by Mathew Mithra Noel, Arindam Banerjee, Yug D. Oswal, Geraldine Bessie Amali D, Venkataraman Muthiah-Nakarajan

The performance of supervised machine learning models is directly related to the quality of the training dataset. In particular, the presence of significantly many outliers in the training data can lead to low accuracy because popular loss function like the Mean Squared Error (MSE) assign very high importance to large errors. The Mean Absolute Error (MAE) loss assigns equal importance to all errors and is most robust to outliers, but suffers from being non-differentiable at the origin. MAE also has large derivative values close to its minimum leading to instability and oscillations during training. Thus differentiable approximations to MAE namely Huber and Log-Cosh losses were introduced for robust regression tasks. This paper introduces two new infinitely differentiable loss functions that more closely approximate the MAE loss and provide improved performance on regression tasks with significantly many outliers in the training dataset. A comparison of the performance of regression models with different loss functions on a wide variety of benchmarks and datasets is presented to demonstrate the superior performance of the Square Root Loss (SRL) and Smooth Mean Absolute Error (SMAE) losses proposed in this paper. The SRL loss is shown to be strictly convex and the SMAE loss is shown to be strictly quasi-convex. Given the fundamental importance of linear regression, two new robust linear regression models are presented.

摘要：監督式機器學習模型的性能與訓練數據集的質量直接相關。<lb/>特別是，訓練數據中存在大量異常值可能導致低準確度，因為像均方誤差（MSE）這樣的常用損失函數對大誤差賦予了非常高的重要性。<lb/>均絕對誤差（MAE）損失對所有誤差賦予相等的重要性，並且對異常值最為穩健，但在原點處存在不可微性。<lb/>MAE在其最小值附近的導數值也很大，導致訓練過程中的不穩定性和振盪。<lb/>因此，為了穩健的回歸任務，引入了對MAE的可微近似，即Huber和Log-Cosh損失。<lb/>本文介紹了兩種新的無限可微損失函數，這些函數更接近於MAE損失，並在訓練數據集中存在大量異常值的回歸任務中提供了改進的性能。<lb/>為了展示本文提出的平方根損失（SRL）和光滑均絕對誤差（SMAE）損失的優越性能，對使用不同損失函數的回歸模型在各種基準和數據集上的性能進行了比較。<lb/>SRL損失被證明是嚴格凸的，而SMAE損失則被證明是嚴格準凸的。<lb/>考慮到線性回歸的基本重要性，本文提出了兩種新的穩健線性回歸模型。

##### **NL2Scratch: An Executable Benchmark and Evaluation for Block-Based Programming**
2606.22061v1 by Heejin Do, Alexandre Ballenghien, Yang Wu, April Yi Wang

Block-based programming environments such as Scratch are widely used in early programming education, yet natural-language-to-code (NL2Code) research has focused primarily on text-based languages. Scratch programs are event-driven, visually compositional, and distributed across concurrent scripts, making conventional NL2Code assumptions and evaluation insufficient. We introduce NL2Scratch, an executable benchmark for natural-language-to-Scratch generation comprising 311,648 parser-valid NL--program pairs, whose program side is extracted from real Scratch projects and paired with semantically aligned NL descriptions. For reliable evaluation beyond surface overlap, we propose Semantic Alignment Consistency (SAC), an interpretable slot-level metric for measuring semantic agreement between descriptions and programs. With SAC, we construct a semantically validated pool of 23,594 examples, and a slot-balanced 800 diagnostic benchmark. Experiments across instruction-tuned and fine-tuned LLMs reveal a notable gap between lexical similarity and semantic alignment: models achieving token-level F1 above 0.93 often fail to attain perfect SAC, particularly on longer examples. Errors concentrate on operational slots like actions, conditions, and numeric arguments, exposing failure modes largely invisible under conventional metrics.

摘要：區塊式編程環境如 Scratch 在早期編程教育中被廣泛使用，但自然語言轉代碼 (NL2Code) 的研究主要集中在基於文本的語言上。Scratch 程式是事件驅動的、視覺組合的，並且分佈在並行的腳本中，這使得傳統的 NL2Code 假設和評估不足。我們介紹 NL2Scratch，這是一個可執行的基準，用於自然語言到 Scratch 的生成，包含 311,648 對解析器有效的 NL--程式對，其程式部分來自真實的 Scratch 項目，並與語義對齊的 NL 描述配對。為了在表面重疊之外進行可靠的評估，我們提出了語義對齊一致性 (SAC)，這是一種可解釋的槽級指標，用於測量描述與程式之間的語義一致性。通過 SAC，我們構建了一個語義驗證的 23,594 個示例的池，以及一個槽平衡的 800 個診斷基準。在針對指令調整和微調的 LLMs 進行的實驗中，顯示出詞彙相似性和語義對齊之間的顯著差距：達到 0.93 以上的令牌級 F1 的模型通常無法獲得完美的 SAC，特別是在較長的示例中。錯誤集中在操作槽上，如動作、條件和數值參數，揭示了在傳統指標下幾乎不可見的失敗模式。

##### **Gradient-Descent Steps to Success over Mean Accuracy: A Paradigm Shift for ML**
2606.22053v1 by Riccardo Poli, Ahmet Yilmaz

Traditional evaluation of machine learning (ML) models typically focuses on achieving the maximum possible accuracy irrespective of the computational cost. In this article, we propose a paradigm shift towards evaluating performance based on computational effort-explicitly defined here as the total number of gradient descent steps required to reach an acceptable level of accuracy with high probability. Building upon the concept of computational effort originally introduced by Koza for Genetic Programming, we extend this metric to any ML model trained via gradient descent. Furthermore, we demonstrate that minimising this effort acts as a novel form of Automatic Machine Learning (AutoML). By evaluating it across 11 diverse ML models and five standard classification datasets, we uncover significant insights into the dynamics of gradient-based learning. Our findings reveal that optimal hyper-parameters consistently favour unusually large learning rates. Crucially, we demonstrate that the rapid, aggressive landscape traversal enabled by these large rates not only promotes generalisation-as seen in phenomena like superconvergence-but also statistically minimises the expected computational effort for training. Furthermore, we identify distinct phase transitions in the optimal search strategy: while a single training run suffices for lower accuracy targets, reaching a model's performance limit requires a dramatic shift towards conducting numerous independent, short restarts. Finally, we illustrate how this effort-based paradigm provides a robust framework for model selection, allowing practitioners to choose optimal algorithms based on the difficulty of a problem as perceived by different models for a given target accuracy, or to maximise the achievable accuracy for a fixed budget of gradient descent steps.

摘要：傳統的機器學習（ML）模型評估通常專注於實現最大的準確性，而不考慮計算成本。在本文中，我們提出了一種範式轉變，將性能評估基於計算努力——在此明確定義為達到可接受的準確性所需的總梯度下降步驟數。基於Koza最初為遺傳編程引入的計算努力概念，我們將此指標擴展到任何通過梯度下降訓練的ML模型。此外，我們展示了最小化這一努力作為一種新型的自動機器學習（AutoML）。通過在11種多樣的ML模型和五個標準分類數據集上進行評估，我們揭示了基於梯度的學習動態的重要見解。我們的研究結果顯示，最佳超參數始終偏好異常大的學習率。關鍵是，我們證明這些大學習率所促進的快速、激進的地形遍歷不僅促進了泛化——如在超收斂等現象中所見——而且在統計上最小化了訓練的預期計算努力。此外，我們確定了最佳搜索策略中的不同相變化：雖然單次訓練運行對於較低的準確性目標已足夠，但達到模型的性能極限則需要向進行多次獨立的短暫重啟劇烈轉變。最後，我們說明了這一基於努力的範式如何為模型選擇提供一個穩健的框架，使從業者能夠根據不同模型對於給定目標準確性的問題難度來選擇最佳算法，或者在固定的梯度下降步驟預算下最大化可達到的準確性。

##### **When Does a Video-Language Model Stop Watching? Reward Strength Controls the Formation and Reversal of Visual Shortcuts in Multimodal RLVR**
2606.22043v1 by Zekun Xu

Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) is increasingly applied to large vision-language models (LVLMs), yet outcome-only optimization can drive a model to stop attending to the video and instead exploit linguistic priors -- a failure we call a visual shortcut. While the existence of such perception bypass is by now documented, how it forms, whether it can be undone, and when intervention still helps remain open. We treat the strength of a grounding penalty, lambda, as a control knob and characterize the formation-reversal dynamics of visual shortcuts along the training time axis. On a held-out, out-of-distribution diagnostic set, we find: (i) a sharp onset -- shortcut reliance emerges abruptly over a narrow window of optimization steps and is robust across random seeds; (ii) a monotone dose-response -- increasing lambda progressively suppresses the shortcut, and at an intermediate dose the trajectory first forms and then reverses the shortcut, exposing a hysteresis-like asymmetry between acquiring and removing it; and (iii) a critical intervention window -- applying the penalty before onset arrests shortcut formation, whereas the same penalty applied after consolidation is markedly less effective. Together these results recast visual-shortcut collapse not as a binary defect but as a controllable, time-dependent, and asymmetric process, with direct implications for when and how strongly to regularize multimodal RLVR.

摘要：強化學習與可驗證獎勵（RLVR）越來越多地應用於大型視覺-語言模型（LVLMs），然而僅依賴結果的優化可能驅使模型停止關注視頻，並轉而利用語言先驗——這種失敗我們稱之為視覺捷徑。儘管這種感知繞過的存在現在已被記錄，但它是如何形成的、是否可以逆轉，以及何時干預仍然是開放的問題。我們將基準懲罰的強度 lambda 視為控制旋鈕，並描述視覺捷徑在訓練時間軸上的形成-逆轉動態。在一個保留的、分佈外的診斷集上，我們發現：（i）急劇的開始——捷徑依賴在狹窄的優化步驟窗口中突然出現，並且在隨機種子之間是穩健的；（ii）單調劑量反應——增加 lambda 逐步抑制捷徑，在中等劑量時，軌跡首先形成然後逆轉捷徑，暴露出獲得和移除之間的滯後性不對稱；以及（iii）關鍵干預窗口——在開始之前施加懲罰可以阻止捷徑形成，而在鞏固之後施加相同的懲罰則明顯效果較差。這些結果共同將視覺捷徑崩潰重新詮釋為一個可控的、時間依賴的和不對稱的過程，而不是一個二元缺陷，對於何時以及多強烈地對多模態 RLVR 進行正則化具有直接的啟示。

##### **Nous: A Predictive World Model for Long-Term Agent Memory**
2606.22030v1 by Pranav Singh

We present Nous, a novel agent memory architecture grounded in the principle that knowledge is prediction, not storage. Rather than persisting facts as database records, vector embeddings, or knowledge-graph triples, Nous maintains a predictive world model: a collection of categorical probability distributions, called dimensions, one per entity-attribute pair observed in conversation. Each incoming observation is scored by its information-theoretic surprise S = -log2 P(obs | D), and the distribution is updated via a closed-form Bayesian posterior. The primary stored artifact is the delta, a record of the shift from prior to posterior belief, rather than the fact itself. Forgetting emerges naturally as entropy decay toward the uniform distribution, and identity resolution is handled through mutual information between entity dimension sets. Evaluated on the LoCoMo long-term conversational memory benchmark across ten conversations (1,540 questions) using GPT-4o-mini as backbone, Nous achieves F1 of 63.50 (single-hop), 55.32 (multi-hop), 58.57 (temporal), and 62.50 (open-domain). Against A-MEM's self-reported GPT-4o-mini numbers, Nous shows substantial gains in three of four categories, though we note that independent citations of A-MEM's results disagree with each other on category assignment, a reproducibility issue we discuss openly rather than resolve unilaterally. We additionally compare against BeliefMem, a concurrently developed system built on the same core premise of belief-based rather than deterministic memory; on the same benchmark and backbone, Nous's self-reported numbers exceed BeliefMem's self-reported numbers on all four categories, though we flag several uncontrolled differences between the two evaluation pipelines that prevent this from being a fully controlled comparison. Nous requires no external vector database or graph engine.

摘要：我們提出了Nous，一種新穎的代理記憶架構，基於知識是預測而非存儲的原則。Nous並不是將事實持久化為資料庫記錄、向量嵌入或知識圖譜三元組，而是維持一個預測世界模型：一組類別概率分佈，稱為維度，每個維度對應於在對話中觀察到的實體-屬性對。每個進來的觀察都根據其信息論驚訝度 S = -log2 P(obs | D) 進行評分，並通過封閉形式的貝葉斯後驗進行更新。主要存儲的物件是增量，記錄從先前信念到後驗信念的轉變，而不是事實本身。遺忘自然地表現為熵衰減至均勻分佈，身份解析則通過實體維度集之間的互信息進行處理。在LoCoMo長期對話記憶基準上，使用GPT-4o-mini作為骨幹，Nous在十次對話（1,540個問題）中達到了63.50（單跳）、55.32（多跳）、58.57（時間）和62.50（開放領域）的F1分數。與A-MEM自報的GPT-4o-mini數據相比，Nous在四個類別中的三個類別顯示出顯著增益，儘管我們注意到A-MEM結果的獨立引用在類別分配上存在不一致，這是一個我們公開討論而非單方面解決的可重複性問題。我們還與BeliefMem進行比較，這是一個同時開發的系統，建立在基於信念而非決定性記憶的相同核心前提上；在相同的基準和骨幹上，Nous自報的數據在所有四個類別中均超過BeliefMem的自報數據，儘管我們標記了兩個評估管道之間的幾個未控制差異，這使得這無法成為一個完全控制的比較。Nous不需要外部向量資料庫或圖形引擎。

##### **RARM: Confidence-Gated Progress Reward Modeling for RL in Manipulation**
2606.22027v1 by Pengzhi Yang, Xinyu Wang, Pengyu Jing, Kehan Wen, Yiduo Qu, Zhenhao Huang, Minghao Fu, Xin Liu, Yaheng Shen, Fan Shi

Reinforcement learning for robot manipulation is often bottlenecked by reward design, especially in long-horizon tasks: sparse success rewards provide weak supervision, while hand-crafted dense rewards are tedious to design and generalize poorly across tasks. Progress-based reward models offer a promising alternative by estimating how far an observation has advanced toward task completion, but existing approaches often require task-specific demonstrations or progress labels, and can assign high rewards to visually plausible but physically incorrect states. We introduce the Reference-Anchored Reward Model (RARM), a lightweight visual comparator that converts a single successful demonstration into a dense, progress-aware reward. RARM is trained once on general-purpose videos with a contrastive temporal objective, requiring no robot-specific data, task-specific reward labels, or per-task reward engineering. At deployment, RARM matches rollout clips to reference clips and rewards only confident forward progress, suppressing uncertain matches that may otherwise produce false-positive rewards. Across 9 simulated manipulation tasks from LIBERO and MetaWorld and 4 real-world tasks, RARM achieves the best overall success rates in subsequent RL training, with particularly large gains on long-horizon tasks such as cloth folding, where unreliable progress estimates are especially harmful.

摘要：強化學習在機器人操作中常常受到獎勵設計的瓶頸，尤其是在長期任務中：稀疏的成功獎勵提供了微弱的監督，而手工設計的密集獎勵則設計繁瑣且在任務間的泛化效果不佳。基於進展的獎勵模型通過估計觀察在任務完成方面的進展程度提供了一個有前途的替代方案，但現有的方法通常需要特定於任務的示範或進展標籤，並且可能會將高獎勵分配給在視覺上合理但在物理上不正確的狀態。我們介紹了參考錨定獎勵模型（RARM），這是一種輕量級的視覺比較器，將單一成功示範轉換為密集的、進展感知的獎勵。RARM 在通用視頻上進行了一次訓練，使用對比時間目標，無需任何特定於機器人的數據、特定於任務的獎勵標籤或每個任務的獎勵工程。在部署時，RARM 將回放片段與參考片段匹配，僅對自信的前進進展給予獎勵，抑制可能產生假陽性獎勵的不確定匹配。在來自 LIBERO 和 MetaWorld 的 9 個模擬操作任務以及 4 個現實世界任務中，RARM 在隨後的強化學習訓練中達到了最佳的整體成功率，尤其在像摺衣服這樣的長期任務中取得了特別大的增益，因為不可靠的進展估計特別有害。

##### **Cluster-Specific Localized Drift Detection for Efficient Batch Model Adaptation under Controlled Distribution Shift**
2606.22026v1 by Ignacio Cabrera Martin, Marcello Trovati, Almas Baimagambetov, Nikolaos Polatidis

Machine learning systems deployed in dynamic environments frequently operate under nonstationary data distributions, where controlled distribution shift can progressively degrade predictive performance. However, many widely used tabular benchmark datasets lack explicit temporal structure, limiting reproducible evaluation of drift adaptation methods. This work proposes a cluster-induced distribution shift simulation framework that transforms static tabular datasets into controlled evolving data streams through structured perturbations across featurespace partitions. Using this framework, six adaptation strategies are systematically evaluated: static learning, sliding-window retraining, global ADWIN retraining, cluster-local ADWIN retraining, random subspace drift detection, and feature-partitioned drift detection. 摘要：機器學習系統在動態環境中部署時，經常在非穩態數據分佈下運行，在這種情況下，受控的分佈變化可能會逐漸降低預測性能。<lb/>然而，許多廣泛使用的表格基準數據集缺乏明確的時間結構，限制了漂移適應方法的可重複評估。<lb/>本研究提出了一種基於聚類誘導的分佈變化模擬框架，通過在特徵空間分區中進行結構性擾動，將靜態表格數據集轉換為受控的演變數據流。<lb/>利用此框架，系統地評估了六種適應策略：靜態學習、滑動窗口再訓練、全局ADWIN再訓練、聚類本地ADWIN再訓練、隨機子空間漂移檢測和特徵分區漂移檢測。<lb/>在五個基準數據集上進行了實驗，涵蓋了分類和回歸任務，使用了包括線性模型、k-最近鄰、樹集成、提升方法和自適應在線學習者在內的多樣預測模型系列。

##### **Channel Location Constrains the Auditability of Subliminal Learning**
2606.22019v1 by Tamas Madl

Subliminal learning lets a student inherit a teacher's hidden trait from distillation data that never names it. We ask when such transfer can be audited before training. The answer is not model identity or scale alone, but channel location: the carrier through which the trait reaches the student. We find three regimes. In a controlled initialization-dependent body channel, a pre-training screen works. Coverage, the cosine between the student's initial distillation update and the teacher's fine-tuning displacement, predicts held-out transfer (Spearman $ρ\approx 0.95$; AUROC 0.997). In pretrained language models, masked single-token traits instead ride convergent vocabulary geometry. This channel is initialization-independent, so initialization-alignment screens, including coverage, are not mechanistic; the useful handles are post-hoc detection and targeted mitigation. Even when a single-token named entity is removed from the loss, the student's held-out probability for that entity rises to 0.40 on average ($\sim 2500\times$), and a related semantic class transfers. In an untied-head model, orthogonalizing the trait's output row against entangled neighbours collapses leakage, while equal-size random-subspace edits do not. Thus removing a target string from distillation labels does not remove the corresponding preference: neighbouring tokens can carry it. Finally, conditional behaviours can route through the network body. For sycophancy, with agreement and correction markers masked from the loss, transfer reaches about 0.63 of the teacher's effect, localizes to body computation, and evades four audits across two model families. We scope this as masked transfer of a condition-present policy. Channel location is necessary for deciding which audits can be sound. It is not a deployment-ready screen: an audit used outside its carrier regime can give false assurance.

摘要：潛意識學習讓學生從未明言的蒸餾數據中繼承教師的隱藏特徵。我們詢問在訓練之前，這種轉移何時可以被審計。答案不僅僅是模型的身份或規模，而是通道位置：特徵到達學生的載體。我們發現三種情況。在受控的初始化依賴體通道中，預訓練篩選有效。覆蓋率，即學生的初始蒸餾更新與教師的微調位移之間的餘弦，預測保留的轉移（Spearman $ρ\approx 0.95$；AUROC 0.997）。在預訓練語言模型中，掩碼單個標記特徵則依賴於收斂的詞彙幾何。這個通道是與初始化無關的，因此初始化對齊篩選，包括覆蓋率，並不是機械性的；有用的手段是事後檢測和有針對性的減輕。即使從損失中移除單個標記命名實體，該實體的學生保留概率平均上升至0.40（$\sim 2500\times$），並且相關的語義類別會轉移。在未綁定頭模型中，將特徵的輸出行與糾纏的鄰居正交化可以消除洩漏，而相等大小的隨機子空間編輯則無法做到。因此，從蒸餾標籤中移除目標字符串並不會消除相應的偏好：鄰近的標記可以攜帶它。最後，條件行為可以通過網絡體路由。對於諂媚，當協議和修正標記從損失中掩蓋時，轉移達到教師效果的約0.63，定位於體計算，並在兩個模型系列中逃避四次審計。我們將此範疇視為條件存在政策的掩碼轉移。通道位置對於決定哪些審計可以是可靠的至關重要。這不是一個準備好部署的篩選：在其載體範疇外使用的審計可能會給出虛假的保證。

##### **Benchmarking Large Language Models for Grapheme-to-Phoneme Conversion: A Japanese Case Study**
2606.22009v1 by Tomoki Koriyama

Grapheme-to-phoneme (G2P) conversion is essential for controllable and robust text-to-speech, and large language models (LLMs), with broad linguistic knowledge, offer a promising approach. We benchmarked over 30 LLMs on Japanese G2P, comparing them with conventional morphological analyzers on 3000 manually annotated sentences. We evaluated two prompting strategies: a parse mode, where the LLM performs morphological analysis followed by rule-based kana conversion, and a direct mode, where the LLM directly predicts kana readings. The results show that model size, version, and Japanese-specialized training are key factors, with the best LLMs achieving kana character error rate below 0.52\% vs. the best conventional tool (1.03\%). Parse mode outperforms direct mode for most models, as rule-based post-processing relieves the LLM of handling complex pronunciation rules. We also show that feeding LLM-predicted kana into a kana-input TTS yields better pronunciation than end-to-end TTS.

摘要：字素到音素（G2P）轉換對於可控且穩健的文本到語音至關重要，而擁有廣泛語言知識的大型語言模型（LLMs）提供了一種有前景的方法。<lb/>我們在日語G2P上對超過30個LLM進行了基準測試，並將它們與3000個手動標註的句子上的傳統形態分析器進行比較。<lb/>我們評估了兩種提示策略：解析模式，其中LLM執行形態分析，然後進行基於規則的假名轉換，以及直接模式，其中LLM直接預測假名讀音。<lb/>結果顯示，模型大小、版本和日語專業訓練是關鍵因素，最佳LLM的假名字符錯誤率低於0.52\%，而最佳傳統工具為1.03\%。<lb/>對於大多數模型來說，解析模式的表現優於直接模式，因為基於規則的後處理減輕了LLM處理複雜發音規則的負擔。<lb/>我們還顯示，將LLM預測的假名輸入假名輸入的TTS，能產生比端到端TTS更好的發音。
